Current Affairs Commentary

Frugality to Save the Poor - Shu 22

丨丨From the German Frugality Movement to Chinese Philanthropy丨丨

The German National Socialist Party recently proposed a religious-like ritual called "Fasting Day," aiming to popularize it nationwide. The money saved from this is intended to relieve the unemployed poor. Whether its effect will be as expected is worth studying. Since the National Socialist Party came to power, it has not yet had a concrete plan for the entire German economic problem. However, the number of unemployed has indeed decreased to more than 3.2 million in the past year. This cannot be said to not be the achievement of the efforts of the National Socialist Party.

Germany is restricted by surrounding countries. Its development in Europe inevitably clashes with the Treaty of Versailles. Even if it wants to develop overseas markets, the world powers have already defined the scope, which is not allowed to be easily touched. In recent years, the international economic struggle has intensified. After the tariff war, it was followed by the currency war, and another strategic economic alliance movement will also advance from theory to practice. Pre-war Germany competed with Britain with its highly developed industry and commerce, but it still could not succeed in the overseas market, let alone today. For example, the monopoly organization of American industry and financial capital is not weaker than Germany, and its natural endowment and geographical advantage are more than ten times that of Germany. However, it is still trapped in a panic frenzy. All methods can only be struggled with. Then the difficulties of Germany can be known without saying it.

Today, Germany uses frugality to help the poor as a temporary emergency solution. It is certainly not impossible. Germans are accustomed to years of struggle. How can they not know that this method is not the end? However, it is limited by the environment. It cannot engage in armed warfare to open up a way out, nor can it obtain foreign markets by peaceful means. Then its internal frugality movement should have considerable significance. However, it is unreliable to rely on this alone to seek a long-term solution. For example, the passive disaster relief and poverty relief methods have been implemented in China for a long time. Not only are there many charitable organizations, but there are also many people who depend on alms for their livelihood. For example, in Beiping, about 300,000 people receive porridge at porridge factories every winter. This is a special reflection of the hardship of the people's livelihood in China. However, this kind of relief is not a fundamental method. It is not enough to help the poor, let alone solve the current predicament. Passive relief measures are difficult to support in the long term, and the heart of compassion can only be triggered occasionally. If it is so long-term, there will be more people who do not work for nothing. It is better to sit and wait for food than to work hard. The rebellions in China have always been due to the failure to solve the problem of people's livelihood adequately. Even the government, known as virtuous and capable, only has ideals and no actual facilities on the issue of people's livelihood. Therefore, the theory of the cycle of governance and chaos has not been thoroughly broken so far. We, in view of the past history, silently observe the current situation, can we not be fearful and think about the fundamental way to remedy it? What is the way to remedy it? The first is to abolish all kinds of harsh taxes and miscellaneous taxes as declared by the central government, and cultivate the vitality of the people. The second rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy. We must actively promote the revival movement. The Rural Relief Committee has decided on four plans, including agricultural finance, agricultural technology, grain regulation and water conservancy, as efforts. We should express the government's determination and sincerity with factual achievements. Third, the frugality movement previously promoted by He Yingqin should be practiced by senior officials and promoted throughout the country. Fourth, we should use scientific and technological development to develop various production undertakings so that the unemployed and people with unstable lives can find a place to live and work.

Executive Yuan Resolves to Allocate Funds to Relieve Refugees in Bandit Areas in Sichuan 23

Xu Fu Concurrently Serves as Director of the Fujian Finance Department

Yao Jun Appointed as Member of the Qinghai Provincial Government

The resolution was to approve the review opinion.

B. Resolutions on Appointments and Removals

It is Said that the People's Sentiments and Engineering Conditions Along the Way are Generally Good

Han spoke, saying that he planned to build large and small gates in Lijin. If the water is high, it can be released to irrigate the alkali land and eliminate river disasters. He then went to Sanbuchen to survey the project. Later, he crossed the river by Xiaojie and inspected the river defense troops. British Navy Overhaul 36

Budget Increased by £2.98 Million

Singapore Naval Base Construction Continues

(London) The British naval budget, announced today, totals £56,550,000, an increase of £2,980,000 compared to last year. According to the Admiralty's explanation, £1,427,000 is for the ordinary construction of new warships, and £1 million was carried over from the 1931 shipbuilding program as it was not fully completed that year. The budget includes the cost of building four new cruisers, eight destroyers, one destroyer flotilla leader, one aircraft carrier, and three submarines. Naval personnel number 92,338, an increase of 2,038. The cost of naval air force equipment increased by £249,000, and naval maintenance costs increased by £1,103,000, as several capital ships require extensive repairs and renovations to extend their lifespan. First Lord of the Admiralty Sir Bolton Eyres Monsell's memorandum stated that, under the London Naval Treaty, Britain is limited in adding or replacing aging cruisers and submarines before 1939. HMS Barham has been modernized, HMS Ramillies is undergoing major repairs, and HMS Malaya will also be renovated. Aircraft launching equipment is under development. New turrets have been installed on twenty-one battleships and cruisers. The Singapore naval base, previously estimated at £7,750,000, has been expanded to £8,693,000. Successful experiments have been conducted on boilers and equipment to reduce weight and volume, and kerosene is being tested on small oil-electric ships. The development of high-speed compressors and combustion engines is also being tested. It was also stated that the 1932 program, which included four cruisers, has been revised to build two larger cruisers. Due to treaty limitations, the fourth cruiser has been discontinued but retains its original status. The First Lord's memorandum also mentioned patrolling against piracy in Dapeng Bay. Notable increases in the naval budget include £249,000 for anti-aircraft equipment for the fleet, £249,000 for repairs and maintenance, £264,000 for special materials, and £1,771,000 for contract work. To achieve the most economical results, construction of the Singapore naval base continues to maintain its effectiveness, so this and future budgets will include this expenditure. (6th, Reuters)

US Army Budget Submitted to House of Representatives 37

Borah Opposes Additional Warship Construction

(Washington) The US Army budget was submitted to the House of Representatives today, requesting $279,541,000 for 130,750 army personnel. The budget falls short of the Chief of Staff's recommendation. According to the Chief of Staff, the United States should have a standing army of 165,000 men and a national guard of 210,000 men. Meanwhile, the House Military Affairs Subcommittee questioned whether the $93 million allocated for military use by the Public Works Administration and the $22 million for civil engineering projects will be used for projects that are absolutely necessary from a national defense standpoint. (5th, Reuters)

(Washington) The House Appropriations Committee and military authorities disagree because Chief of Staff General MacArthur proposed increasing the US regular army from 130,000 to 165,000 men and the National Guard from 190,000 to 210,000 men. This proposal was rejected by the Appropriations Committee. Furthermore, the government requested $349,523,000 for military expenditures for the next year, but the Appropriations Committee only approved $279,541,000. From the public works budget, $7,500,000 was allocated to purchase aircraft and $22,591,000 for aviation expenses. The number of new aircraft requested by military authorities was originally 348, but the Appropriations Committee reduced this to 290 due to currency devaluation. The committee attached a stern report to the budget bill, stating, "There are irregularities in the purchase of aircraft, whether planned or manufactured, which have recently been exposed. The Appropriations Committee is aware of this. Not only in aircraft but also in other purchases, there are irregularities." The Appropriations Committee expressed dissatisfaction with the allocation of funds from public works or civil engineering projects to military expenditures, stating that this method is based on emergency legislation. However, legislative power belongs to Congress, and this special exception should not be prolonged. The Appropriations Committee requested that this power be returned to Congress. The committee report also stated that the use of various supplementary funds has not been seen to greatly benefit national defense. (5th, Havas)

(Washington) The Senate will discuss the $500 million naval construction bill today. Republican Senator Borah declared during preliminary discussions that US arms manufacturers sell some of the arms they manufacture to a certain Eastern country, and if war breaks out between Japan and the United States, American soldiers will be killed by weapons sold by their own country. He also stated that he "does not believe that arms manufacturers can cause such a war, but when war is about to break out, these insatiable people may not abandon the idea of making profits." Mr. Borah opposed the naval construction bill, saying that the warships currently under construction are sufficient and there is no need to build new ones. (5th, Havas)

US President Proposes Reopening World Economic Conference Currency Obstacles Removed Economic Struggle May Be Resolved Special Envoy Sent to Europe for Consultations 39

(Washington) According to sources at the White House today, President Roosevelt may attempt to reconvene the World Economic Conference. It is learned that American diplomat and international affairs expert Mr. Charles will be President Roosevelt's personal special envoy, visiting European countries to gather opinions on reopening the World Economic Conference, as the President believes now may be the time to resolve the economic struggle. Since the collapse of the World Economic Conference on July 27 last year, the European economic situation has changed greatly. The President believes that all countries will be able to make considerable sacrifices to improve the world economic situation. Observers say that the American President's proposal to reopen the conference may finally bring about a resolution to the American proposal. Mr. Hull, the US representative, requested a preliminary date for the reopening of the conference when attending the London Steering Committee, but it failed due to the joint opposition of European representatives. The World Economic Conference opened in London on June 12 last year. Although the representatives each delivered impressive empty words, the conference broke down on July 27. The focal point of the breakdown was the issue of currency stabilization, as France and the gold standard countries demanded the prompt stabilization of international currency values, while the United States strongly rejected everything, expressing opposition to the devaluation of the dollar. Today, the US government's devaluation plan has been implemented, so it is believed that there will be no similar entanglement in the future, and the resumption of talks may produce beneficial results. The only concrete agreement of the World Economic Conference, apart from the short-lived tariff truce, is the recent popular London Silver Agreement. (5th, National News Agency)

(New York) According to today's news, Mr. Charles will depart for England on March 14 on behalf of the Roosevelt administration to investigate the European economic situation. Mr. Charles will spend three months in Europe. He told people today that he has no authority to represent the United States in establishing agreements on currency stability, war debts, or any other issues, but he is free to discuss these issues with European politicians. He knows that Roosevelt wants to know what actions other countries are taking to contribute to the recovery of the world economy. Mr. Charles served as an advisor to Secretary of State Hull during last year's World Economic Conference in London. (5th, Reuters)

Charles' Biography 40

Mr. Charles, former US Ambassador to Rome, has recently been appointed as a special advisor by Secretary of State Hull. The following is a brief biography of Mr. Charles. Mr. Charles is 53 years old this year. During the final years of World War I, from 1917 to 1918, he served as the director of the wartime finance group of the Treasury Department. From 1921 to 1924, he served as the Ambassador to Italy. During his tenure, he led the US delegation to the Genoa and Lausanne conferences in 1922. (The Genoa Conference discussed reparations and European economic recovery, and delegations from Germany and Russia also participated. The Lausanne Conference was the second peace treaty with Turkey after World War I, which established the Treaty of Lausanne, demilitarizing the Dardanelles and Bosphorus straits and entrusting their management to the League of Nations Straits Committee.) Mr. Charles is a prolific writer, with many books and novels on diplomacy and social issues. His articles are frequently published in American newspapers and magazines. (5th, Havas)

Page 10

Roosevelt's Radio Address

A Further Explanation of the Recovery Plan

National Production Needs Reorganization

Controlled Economy Not Contrary to the Constitution

Democracy Has Failed, Implement New System Decisively

(Washington) President Roosevelt, in a radio broadcast address, explained the necessity of reorganizing national production. He stated that from 1919 to 1929, the national economy was like a madman, and no one at that time put forward any plan to avoid the harm of overproduction, nor did anyone seek a way to allow the public to buy things they could not afford. He also said that during these years, the authorities and the people were not invigorated, so that the government's power fell into the hands of some groups, and the purpose of these groups was to seek the self-interest of some classes. As for the economic recovery plan implemented by the current government, its main spirit is to strive for the improvement of the lives of the largest number of people within the greatest possible limit. The method is to increase wages to restore purchasing power, and develop foreign trade to seek a balance between agriculture and industry. In short, under a representative government, the implementation of economic control policies is not contrary to the principles stipulated in the U.S. Constitution. (Fifth, Havas Dispatch)

(Washington) President Roosevelt addressed the staff of the National Recovery Administration today, advocating that the industrial sector should immediately reduce working hours again, so that the unemployed and those who lost their jobs could obtain work with a living wage. President Roosevelt said that this must be done in order to continue the work of revitalizing the country and restoring equilibrium.

Reorganize Production and Exchange Systems President Roosevelt also said that Americans whose annual income is less than $2,000 purchase two-thirds of the goods sold domestically. Therefore, as the wages earned by these people gradually increase, merchants, employers, and investors will eventually be able to increase their income due to increased sales of goods. A year ago, when the business was in decline, we legally took on the system of reorganizing production and exchange, and now we must make this reorganization lasting.

Strive for an Average of Wealth and Power We must never again allow a social situation in which a large proportion of the people exist in a state incompatible with Americanization, and in which the distribution of wealth and power is uneven. The willingness of all parties to participate in this new undertaking is now more evident than before. For example, I recently received a telegram from the American Bankers Association, representing banks across the country, expressing their trust and sincerity and their willingness to support the efforts to revitalize the country. This is proof of this. The structure of American banks is sound, and the position of each bank now in operation is more stable than ever before. The situation has reached a point of extreme liquidity. Gentlemen, try to recall what position the banks were in a year ago today. You all know it. The telegram from the Bankers Association today is clear proof of progress.

Seek Greater Welfare for the People We should consolidate what we have already gained, and resolve to make what we have consolidated beneficial to continued progress, and especially to the greater welfare of the American people. What the National Recovery Administration seeks is to balance our economic system, to maintain our domestic market so that it is rich and large, and to increase the trade between our country and other countries. The government cannot continue to bear the entire burden of unemployment forever. What should be done at present is to enable more people to obtain work. Wherever industrial autonomy fails, the government must act decisively and quickly to prevent its failure.

Industry Regulations Protect Small Industries The industry regulations authorities are the custodians of our industrialists, especially the custodians of our small industrialists. We must establish all kinds of safeguards to avoid the extinction of small industrialists. All industry regulations must stop the competitive methods that squeeze out small industrialists.

Adopt New Systems and Strive for Revival The situation in March 1933 was extremely serious. Many diseases must be treated simultaneously. The purpose is to use American methods to provide this relief, not to imitate the treatments that other countries have tried. President Roosevelt mentioned that the authorities have now adopted communism and collectivism or have adopted fascism and dictatorial systems, saying that American democratic organs have been ineffective for many years, half due to the leaders and half due to the inertia of the people themselves. President Roosevelt also said that most critics comment on the details and methods of the recovery plan, rather than on the recovery plan itself. This can be regarded as satisfactory. The entire purpose of the Recovery Administration is to increase the purchasing power of the people, a conscious and rational benefit, which no one opposes. However, most people are currently in a state of displacement. When there is a question of humanity first and then interests, we cannot allow hesitation. (Fifth, Reuters Dispatch)

Rice Issue: Agricultural and Colonial Ministries Stand in Opposition 56

(Tokyo) The opposition between Agriculture Minister Goto and Colonial Minister Nagai over the issue of importing rice from the colonies has not been resolved. Goto is supported by domestic landlords and political parties, and his attitude is very strong. The Legislative Bureau's compromise plan is not recognized by the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry. This morning, Minister of Railways Tsuchi met with Yamamoto, Takahashi, and Saito in the Diet to meet with Nagai and Goto, and persuaded the two ministers to settle the dispute, but the result was not satisfactory. The opinions of both sides are as follows: A. "Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry Proposal" (1) Clearly stipulate the number of rice grains imported from Taiwan and Korea into the country, and receive special imports into the country from the governments of the two places on a monthly basis. (2) The Korean and Taiwanese governments should purchase surplus rice grains in their localities. (3) If the rice grains purchased by the two governments are to be imported into the country, they should first consult with the Minister of Agriculture and then proceed. (4) The Minister of Agriculture may use the funds from the special accounting of rice grains to purchase the rice grains collected by the two governments. (5) The number of imported rice grains in the third and fourth items cannot exceed the number stipulated in the first item. B. "Ministry of Colonial Affairs Proposal" (1) Do not specially establish a purchasing committee. When using the law to purchase rice grains, the governments of the two colonies must agree with the Minister of Colonial Affairs, the Minister of Finance, and the Minister of Agriculture on the number of rice grains to be purchased. (2) The funds required for purchasing rice grains are determined by the five-minister conference to be 10 million won in Korea and 50 million yuan in Taiwan. In order to achieve the purpose of purchasing, an additional 50 million yuan will be added. (3) The colonial grain rice import combination proposal advocated by the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry cannot agree with treating the colonies unequally for ruling foreign lands. (4) The Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry advocated raising the tariffs on Manchurian millet to prevent imports from Korea into the country. Because it has been raised by 10% last year, it should not be raised again, and Koreans are living in great difficulty. It is not possible to trample on their lives by preventing Korean rice from entering the country. (Sixth, Hualian Dispatch)

French Newspaper Discusses Inevitability of Russo-Japanese War 91

=Japan relies on military force like a hungry tiger descending from the mountains to devour the fattest prey=

=The Russian government is currently contacting friendly nations in order to strengthen its power=

Paris Correspondence: Yan Huiqing, the Chinese ambassador to Russia, recently left Russia to return to China. When passing through Singapore, he made remarks about the inevitability of the Russo-Japanese War. These remarks have attracted considerable attention from the French public, and most French newspapers have used them as material for commentary. The most prominent example is an essay by Robert Poulaine in a Paris magazine, titled "Is the Russo-Japanese War Possible or Certain?" According to Poulaine's opinion, war between the two countries is unavoidable. The main reason he holds is that Japan is currently in an era of rising military power, and the military has a full ambition to annex Manchuria, which Soviet Russia is an obstacle to. Therefore, it must be eliminated. Currently, Japan's army and navy are truly capable of dominating the world. Although the navy is constrained by the London Naval Treaty, it can still compete with the British Navy. The Japanese Emperor, along with army leaders such as Army Minister Araki, has gained the faith of the public and has already become the dictator of the country. Therefore, Japanese soldiers are almost like hungry tigers descending from the mountains, devouring the fattest prey. According to Poulaine's observations in Manchuria, he felt that the Japanese soldiers' endurance was superior to that of soldiers from other countries. Every day, they carry only a small amount of rice, a fish, and a small amount of tea, and walk forty miles without fatigue. Moreover, they have all received considerable education. Within each regiment of 1,500 soldiers, only 15 are illiterate. If we consider each regiment of French soldiers, the ratio is 30% to 35%. Poulaine then mentioned that in August of last year, the entire populations of Tokyo and Yokohama mobilized to practice aerial defense exercises for three days and nights. During the exercises, 25,000 young men and women raised funds from all walks of life, raising no less than 10 million francs for the government. The enthusiasm of the Japanese public for military affairs and their spirit of sacrifice are commendable. The number of volunteers capable of acting as human torpedoes far exceeds the number conscripted. Once the country is in trouble, these torpedoes can explode at any time. What is even more worrying is that the Japanese population increases by one million every year, and the total population has already reached 60 million. For the sake of feeding its 60 million residents, it has no choice but to occupy Manchuria, because Manchuria has no European countries competing with it for new markets, and at the same time it is a storage place for raw materials needed for its national defense.

Since the resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia, Japan has deeply understood that there is little hope for a co-existence agreement between Japan and Russia. Therefore, for the sake of national security, it will later occupy the coastal provinces near Vladivostok and the northern part of Sakhalin Island in order to complete its plan to invade Manchuria.

Poulaine's pessimistic views are deeply sympathized with by the Moscow government. The Moscow government really does not want any war to happen, but deeply feels that it will be threatened by Japan sooner or later. The Moscow government is now changing its policy, preparing to sign non-aggression treaties and trade agreements with "intermediate-level" governments, in order to strengthen its strength against Japan, and so on. (World Press)

Completion of the Lafa-Binjiang Railway Operated by the Japanese (Changchun Correspondence) 92

丨Shortening the transportation route between Northern Manchuria and Japan丨

The Dunhua-Tumen line (that is, the disguised form of the Jihui Railway from Dunhua to Tumen) operated by the Japanese was completed in April last year. The Lafa-Binjiang line was again entrusted to the South Manchuria Railway Company by the Japanese puppet organization and test-run on December 13 last year. The line is 262 kilometers long, starting from Lafa Station on the Jitu Road and ending at Binjiang, the economic center of Northern Manchuria. It crosses the western part of Jilin Province, crosses the Chinese Eastern Railway, and shortens the distance between Binjiang (Harbin), the distribution center for products from Northern Manchuria, and the Japanese mainland. It is also the nerve center of the Northern Manchurian railway network. The distance from Binjiang to Lafa via this road, and then from Lafa to Najin Port in North Korea via the Dunhua-Tumen line, is 207 kilometers shorter than the distance from Harbin south to Dalian. In the past, the shortest route between Northern Manchuria and Japan was 2,020 kilometers from Binjiang to Shimonoseki via the Korean Railway. Now, it is only 1,616 kilometers from Binjiang via the Lafa-Binjiang line to Najin and then to Tsuruga. In other words, the distance from the center of Northern Manchuria to the Japanese mainland is shortened by 396 kilometers with the completion of the Lafa-Binjiang line and the Dunhua-Tumen line. Therefore, the completion of this road has opened a new era in transportation between Northern Manchuria and Japan, and has increased an effective weapon for Japan's military and economic aggression against Manchuria.

Although the total length of the road is only 262 kilometers, there are amazing aspects to its engineering. For example, the Songhua River Railway Bridge at the junction of the road and the Hu-Hai Road is 1.4 kilometers long, which is 31 meters longer than the Chinese Eastern Railway Bridge, which was formerly known as a major project in Northeast China. It is also longer than the Yalu River Bridge. The bridge is a two-story structure, with the upper level for pedestrians and horses, and the lower level for the railway. The construction cost reached 4.2 million yuan. In terms of its scale and form, it can be said to be the first large bridge in the Northeast. In addition, there is a famous Taipingling Tunnel on the road, which is 690 meters long and is also one of the major projects on the line.

The scenery along the line is very different from other railways in the Northeast. The railway meanders along the foothills of the mountains, and the entire line is covered with forests. Therefore, when building the railway, the Japanese specifically cleared 50 meters of land on both sides of the railway, leaving a considerable distance between the trees to serve as natural poles for electric wires. Therefore, today when passing through this place, one only sees small trees of two or three feet, and no longer sees the original forests that were once green and secluded, covering the sky and the sun.

The purpose of the road construction and the purpose of the Japanese to rush to complete it are, on the one hand, to shorten the distance between Northern Manchuria and the Japanese mainland, so as to fully absorb the rich resources of Northern Manchuria. On the other hand, in order to cope with the increasingly tense Russo-Japanese war clouds, Japan is shortening the route for transporting troops, so that troops from the Japanese mainland can quickly reach Northern Manchuria and invade Soviet territory. In addition, the areas along the road were originally areas where our volunteer army hid and emerged. The Japanese rushed to build this road in order to eliminate our volunteer army, which is also one of the reasons.

Since the completion of the road, the Chinese Eastern Railway, which is also known as the lifeline of transportation in Northern Manchuria, has lost its effectiveness due to the shorter distance to the sea. The cities along the line include Wuchang and Lalin. The number of Japanese and Korean farmers who have migrated here is increasing day by day. The temperature along the line is quite low, often reaching minus 30 to 40 degrees Celsius in winter. Therefore, travelers on this road only see the wilderness covered by white snow, merging into one color with the sky.

Chen Jitang Disbands Huang Hechun Brigade 93

=Huang's Brigade was reorganized from the remnants of the 19th Route Army=

=Xu Minghong was arrested in Dapu and executed on the spot=

Guangzhou Correspondence: The 3,000 remnants of the 19th Route Army and Cai Tingkai's guardsmen were previously concentrated in Longyan and surrendered to Guangdong. At that time, Chen Jitang sent Huang Renhuan, the commander of the 1st Independent Division, to reorganize them into the 3rd Independent Brigade, appointing Huang Hechun as the brigade commander, and transferred the brigade back to Guangdong to be stationed on the border for training. Unexpectedly, Chen Jitang recently ordered the 1st Independent Division to disarm Huang Hechun's brigade. After receiving the order, Huang Renhuan disarmed the three regiments of the brigade. It is said that the reason for the brigade being disarmed is that Chen Jitang was ordered to do so by the central government, and that after the brigade was reorganized, it had other intentions, which were discovered by Chen Jitang, so he disbanded it. As for the officers and soldiers of the brigade, Chen immediately telegraphed Huang Renhuan, ordering him to appropriately accommodate the lower-level cadres and officers. Those who wished to join the army were allowed to be sent back to the province at government expense for training and recruitment. It is said that on that day, more than 500 officers of the brigade volunteered to continue serving in the army and were immediately escorted back to the province by personnel from the 1st Independent Division, temporarily stationed in Yantang, to await training. As for the more than 3,000 scattered soldiers of the 19th Route Army who were transported back to Guangzhou by Shantou ship a few days ago, they are currently awaiting distribution in Huangpu. More than 1,000 people have been selected and taken away by various armies, and more than 2,000 people still need to be trained. The authorities have specially established a new recruit training center in the former officers' club in Huangpu, which was established on March 1, to receive and retrain the more than 2,000 scattered soldiers.

Xu Minghong, the former puppet governor of Longting, who participated in the puppet government of Fujian, was a native of Fengshun, Guangdong, and a member of the Third Party. Last year, he was ordered by the Third Party to carry out activities in Fujian. After the collapse of the puppet government of Fujian, Xu disguised himself and fled. When he arrived in Dapu County, Guangdong Province, he was captured by the defense army and detained at the headquarters of the 1st Independent Division. Huang Renhuan submitted a request to Chen Jitang, who executed Xu on the spot and announced Xu's crimes. (March 2)

Hunan Province Has Surplus Grain and Rice 94

He Jian Asks the Central Government to Increase the Tax on Foreign Rice

And Orders All Provinces of Fujian and Guangdong to Implement It Uniformly

Changsha Correspondence: Hunan Province is a traditionally rich area for grain production. In the past, millions of dan were shipped to Shanghai and Hankou every year. In recent years, harvests have been abundant, and the Yangtze River Basin has also experienced bumper harvests. Moreover, large quantities of foreign rice have been shipped to China for dumping, resulting in Hunan rice losing its market. Storage is full and prices are low, which not only puts the rural economy in a desperate situation, but also greatly impacts the financial market. According to reports from the grain and rice industry in Changsha City, since the bumper harvest in the 19th year of the Republic, the grain and rice storage in Changsha City alone has been renewed and then renewed again over the years. There are now more than 2 million dan, which can supply the city's population for two or three years. As a result, the existing grain and rice have goods but no market. The best Tianzihao machine rice only sells for 5.30 or 40 yuan per dan, and the best grain only sells for 2.10 or 20 yuan per dan. The banks and grain merchants that store grain have suffered heavy losses. The Grain Merchants Association has specifically requested the provincial government to find ways to provide relief in two aspects: (1) Increase the tax on foreign rice. The provinces of Fujian and Guangdong have not yet implemented it. According to the investigation, Fujian and Guangdong are the largest markets for foreign rice. If the two provinces are excluded, then the so-called increase in the tax on foreign rice is actually equal to zero. Therefore, the rice shipped from Hunan to Guangzhou for sale has resulted in losses. It is requested that the provincial government telegraph the central government to strictly order the provinces of Fujian and Guangdong to uniformly implement the tax increase on foreign rice, so as to sell off the excess grain in the interior. (2) The grain reserves in Hunan are too abundant, and both the business community and the rural areas are suffering. It is requested that the provincial government contact various banks to invest in purchases and transport them downstream to revitalize the financial market and regulate the rural economy. He Jian, the chairman of the provincial government, will submit it to the provincial affairs meeting on March 2 for detailed discussion. All department heads and committee members believe that it is necessary to provide active relief. It was decided that: 1. The Department of Finance and the Hunan Provincial Bank will temporarily entrust the original 1 million yuan fund for transporting and selling grain and rice to the Grain and Rice Transportation and Sales Committee to purchase and transport 500,000 dan of grain and rice, part of which will be transported and sold downstream, and part of which will be stored in warehouses for famine relief. In addition, contact the banking community in Changsha to invest in transporting and selling grain and rice. 2. Telegraph the central government and Chairman Chiang to implement an increase in the import tax on foreign rice, and order the provinces of Fujian and Guangdong to implement it uniformly. He Jian's telegram to the central government is as follows: To Wang Jingwei, President of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, and Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Finance, and Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry: According to the Changsha Grain and Rice Industry Association's report, the investigation found that the tax on foreign rice has not been implemented in Fujian and Guangdong, and the dumping of foreign rice is becoming more and more serious. Domestic grain and rice have nowhere to sell, and farmers and merchants are suffering. Please forward to the central government to strictly order all provinces of Fujian and Guangdong to implement it uniformly by a certain date, etc. The investigation found that the dumping of foreign rice hinders the sales of domestic grain and rice and has a huge impact. If the import tax is not implemented uniformly, affecting the whole country with one corner, then domestic agricultural products will never have a market, the rural areas will collapse, the business community will wither, and the foundations of the country will be shaken. According to the previous situation, I specially telegraph to request your examination and approval to increase the import tax rate on foreign rice, and quickly order all provinces of Fujian and Guangdong to follow it uniformly, etc. He Jian, Chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government, respectfully submits. (March 3)

Recent Developments in Jiangbei Construction 95

丨丨Director Shen Talks About the Inspection Process丨丨

Zhenjiang Correspondence: Shen Baixian, Director of the Jiangsu Construction Department, Zhao Dihua, Director of the Finance Department, and Committee Member Yu Bingtang recently went to Jiangbei to inspect the party and government and construction in various counties. Director Shen and others returned to the province yesterday. According to reports, the inspection process is as follows: I have always believed that Jiangsu's construction focuses on Jiangbei, and Jiangbei's construction focuses on water conservancy. Therefore, Director Zhao, Committee Member Yu, and I resolutely embarked on a trip to inspect Jiangbei. We departed on February 22 and returned to the province yesterday, a total of nine days. We visited eleven counties, including Donghai, Guanyun, Ganyu, Shuyang, Lianshui, Siyang, Suqian, Huaiyin, Huaian, and Gaoyou. Although the construction in various counties has not made any special progress due to tight funding, the need to develop water conservancy and build roads has gradually been recognized by the public. The most important findings of this inspection are the following three: The first is the Lianyungang Project. Lianyungang is located at the eastern end of the Longhai Railway, about 20 li east of Xugou in Guanyun County. The terrain is very dangerous, with islands lying across the sea from east to west, forming a natural barrier. The project is sponsored by the Longhai Railway Engineering Bureau and undertaken by the Dutch Port Management Company. The original plan was very complete, but due to funding constraints, it was temporarily decided to complete only a part of it. The initial project will be completed within this year. The tide direction is from east to west, so the initial plan was to build a breakwater at the eastern end, which is 1,000 meters long. Currently, 500 meters have been built. Two new-style wharves are being built to the west of the dike, and one-third of them have been completed. The Longhai Railway has been extended from Xugou to Laoyao, with mountain drilling and stone blasting, and the project is extremely large. The Longhai Railway runs across northern Jiangsu, southern Henan, and directly to western Gansu. After the completion of the eastern port project, seagoing vessels with a draft of 6 meters can sail in the port all year round. The convenience of combined water and land transportation is self-evident. The goods from the interior of our country can be imported and exported from here, which is not only related to the development of the Northwest. The second is the development of the Xugou commercial market. After the completion of Lianyungang, commercial development is just around the corner, so the development of the new city of Xugou should not be delayed, so that it can complement each other. The third is the Sixitang River project. Since the provincial government decided to carry out the Sixitang River project, an engineering office was established in Huaiyin in mid-December last year to actively prepare. The levee construction work on various sections has already started one after another. The farmers near the river are very enthusiastic about the work due to their personal interests. Even though they had to stop work for only a few days due to the old customs of the New Year, when I visited the various work sections, the actual labor force in each section totaled nearly 30,000 people. Later, the number of people can gradually increase, the weather can gradually become warmer, and the work will progress more rapidly. The river dams in the sections where excavation is required have been completed and built, and the accumulated water has been completely drained. The tools for excavating sandbags are also well-equipped and arranged. The excavation project can also be started at the same time within a few days. The entire project can be completed as scheduled before May. (April 4)

Songjiang Water Patrol Team Captures Thugs 96

The Fangjiaxia area of Fenjing Cemetery was formerly a gathering place for reactionaries. The number of honest and good people who have been poisoned by them is countless. Fang Xiuyun of Fangjiaxia once served as the detective chief of the Fenjing Security Regiment. He forcibly borrowed and extorted money in the countryside. After the case was discovered, he was arrested, and the court sentenced him to imprisonment. He appealed to the High Court. Because the victim dared not identify him, he was declared innocent and released. Unexpectedly, after being released and returning to his hometown, he relapsed. Fang cut off the wooden handle of a discarded gun, shortened the barrel, and installed it, making it look like a box cannon. He used this homemade gun to threaten the villagers, such as forcibly borrowing money ranging from 70 to 80 yuan to 20 to 30 yuan, and forcibly taking grain, causing the villagers to be unable to pay rent. There were more than 20 families who were victimized. The victims did not dare to bear grudges because the losses were very small, so they all endured in silence. After the captain of the Water Patrol Team, Fei Gongxia, learned about the matter, he supervised the captain Luo Shutang to go to the countryside and arrest Fang, and seized the fake gun. He has already been taken back to the team headquarters for interrogation.

Suzhou Zhenya Resolves Dismissal Dispute 97

The Cangjie Zhenya Weaving Factory laid off more than 100 workers in order to shut down the hand-weaving department. The workers were unwilling to be laid off and caused trouble to the factory for no reason, resulting in a dispute. The county government convened a mediation meeting again yesterday (the 6th) at 10:00 AM. Representatives from all parties concerned attended. It was decided that the dismissal was decided. As for the issue of severance pay, in addition to the 24 yuan per person paid by the factory, the county government and the county party department will subsidize 6 yuan per person. The severance pay will be issued today (the 7th), and the dismissal will be implemented.

Wuxi Rice Industry's Increased Commission Still Difficult to Resolve 98

The rice and bean merchants in Wuxi and Wu counties changed the original 99% commission to 98.4%. The Bengbu grain merchants actively opposed the seal and elected representatives Li Peisheng, Sun Yuanfu, Hu Hanqing, and Qian Xiaosheng to come to Wuxi for negotiation the day before yesterday. Lin Yibao, chairman of the Wujin Rice and Bean Industry Association, and Lin Junbao, executive director of the county chamber of commerce, also arrived in Wuxi at the same time and invited Zhao Zixin, Feng Yunxiang, and others from the Wuxi Rice and Bean Industry to have a discussion at the county chamber of commerce. The Bengbu representatives said that the Bengbu merchants have suffered heavy losses due to the sharp drop in grain prices in recent years and are seeking ways to provide relief. However, the sudden increase in the commission by the two counties of Wuxi and Wu makes it even more difficult for grain merchants to maintain. If a satisfactory solution cannot be reached, they will have to submit a request to the provincial government to strictly order a halt. On the one hand, they will have to transport soybeans directly to Shanghai for sale. Later, Qian Sunqing, the executive director of the chamber of commerce, earnestly persuaded both parties not to go to extremes and decided that today (the 7th) the chamber of commerce would invite representatives from the Bengbu merchants to visit Taihu Lake in order to negotiate together.

Telephone Company Expands Electrical Equipment 99

The telephone company in this county was founded in the first year of the Republic of China by Yang Hanxi and others. Initially, only merchants in the urban area installed telephones to facilitate communication. However, it was not yet widespread, so there were only a few hundred telephones in the entire city. In recent years, the company's business has been very developed, with the number of telephones increasing to more than 1,300. Various towns in the rural areas have also installed them. Recently, Mr. Yang purchased 120 more telephones from the United States for the purpose of expanding business, specifically for use by merchants in the urban area. At the same time, he ordered the mechanics to actively set up telephone lines, which are now ready for users to gradually install. According to someone from the company, the telephones in the urban area have had a slight surplus in recent years, but the cost of the telephone lines is very high. Once they are damaged, the repair costs are also not light. In the rural telephone areas, there is no profit to be made, because the telephone charges are the same as in the urban area, but the telephone poles are placed very far apart, and repairs are not easy, and the losses are even greater. Currently, the telephone poles and lines in Zhangjingqiao in the seventh district have been damaged and should be replaced immediately, but the cost is too high, so it has to be postponed for the time being.

Major Fire in Qianqiu Lane, Changzhou 100

Qianqiu Lane in the city of Wujin is a bustling market. In the middle section is the Deyuanchang Paper Store, which has been open for many years. However, its business has been sluggish in recent years, and it has been managed by the late Wang Shaohua. Unexpectedly, at around 8:00 PM on the 5th, a fire suddenly broke out in the storage room on the second floor of the store. At that time, the westerly wind was strong. In a few minutes, it had broken through the roof and spread to the neighboring Zhenda Rice Store. By the time the bell rang to warn the police, the fire brigades from various districts rushed to the scene, and the fire had also spread to the opposite Xuyuanxing Iron Shop and Yilong Vegetarian Restaurant. The fire was so intense that it was rare in recent years in this city. At that time, the river water was shallow and difficult to use. After the firefighters tried their best to put out the fire, it was extinguished after about an hour. However, the nearby electric poles were burned down, and most of the lights and telephone users in the entire city were in a dark world and could not make calls. Afterwards, the company sent many craftsmen to try to repair them. It was not until around 9:00 PM that the repairs were completed. Sun Meicheng, the chief of the first sub-bureau of public security, sent the police to summon the store owner for questioning because the origin of the fire at Deyuanchang was unknown, but the store owner had disappeared.

Jiangyin Provincial Order Merges Autonomous Regions 101

County Magistrate Bao, in accordance with the provincial order, reorganized the autonomous regions. Any areas with a land area of less than 5,000 square li may not exceed eight districts. The area of Cheng County is only 2,970 square li, with a population of 750,000. Yesterday (the 4th), the meeting decided to merge the original fourteen districts into seven districts and elected Secretary Bao Siren, District Heads Cheng Hongrui and Yu Weiqing, Section Chief Luo Zhibin, and Property Director Chen Zhongda as design committee members to discuss the methods and charts, etc., hand them over to the district heads' meeting for approval, and submit them for implementation.

Zhenjiang-Chengjiang Road Begins Construction 102

The Zhenjiang-Chengjiang section of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway has already started construction of the roadbed in Zhenjiang and Jiangyin counties. The section in Wujin is being demolished to remove obstacles. The bridge and culvert engineering on this road is quite large. The tenders were initially divided into six sections and started last month on the 22nd. The Department has approved four companies, including Minsheng Construction Company, Zhonghua Industrial Company, Jianxing Company, and Hushengji, each to get one section, and Xiehe Company to get two sections. The contracts have been signed, and they have started transporting materials and are actively starting construction.

Repairing and Dredging Rural Ditches 103

The Ditch Works Committee of this county, seeing that the busy farming season is approaching, is making great efforts to advance the work. The committee's planned project, the embankment from Cuijia Bridge to Yonggu Township, is already half completed and will be fully completed in a week. The bridge body of Cuijia Bridge, which has been in disrepair for many years and is also an important transportation route, is currently being designed and a wooden bridge will be rebuilt. The farmland in the east of the township is relatively fertile. The committee originally planned to dredge the ditches, but after receiving opinions from enthusiastic locals such as Liu Zhixian, they believed that opening ditches would be more effective than dredging. Construction has now begun on excavating six ditches, divided into two teams of about seventy or eighty people. They are 820 zhang long, and 2400 fang in volume, with the narrowest being six chi and the widest being two zhang, and a depth of about four or five chi, to allow water to flow. One ditch has already been excavated and will be completed soon. More than a thousand mu of farmland will benefit. The committee will subsidize each fang with two jiao and two fen. Liu, considering the difficulty of the work, plans to increase it to two jiao and five fen. All the excavation costs are advanced by him.

Yangzhou Audit Office Collects Salt Certificate Surtax 104

The Jiandu County, which has been plagued for quite some time, the education, public security, and charity salt certificate surtax, regarding the transportation aspect, is already being implemented by the Huaibei Audit Sub-Office for collection, which is remitted through Yangzhou Shanghai Bank for transfer. However, apart from these three items, all other matters, such as the merchant guild's subsidy, are not being handled. As for the sailing transportation portion and the celery tax, they are still being collected in Yangzhou. It is heard that it has been implemented separately since March 1st.

Nantong Sandbar Land Grab Unpaid 105

The provincial government investigated and found that Xu Daochun, a sandbar operator in Nantong, occupied 1,500 mu of滩田 in the sixth and seventh圩 in Changyin Sandbar. All were confiscated and ordered the county government to recover. Xu resisted and refused to pay and was detained, but stated that the land in the sixth and seventh圩 did not belong to him and requested release. County Magistrate Cheng stated that this case had been decided by the provincial government, and Xu Daochun must sign a guarantee to hand over the occupied land before bail would be granted. This was rejected.

Major Murder-for-Money Case in Hangzhou 106

Li Chuhua, a 25-year-old accountant from Ningxiang, Hunan, stationed at the Third Branch Office of the Quzhou Security Corps, led his orderly, Wang Qinggen, 30 years old, also from Hunan, from Quzhou to the provincial capital on the morning of the 4th of this month. They stayed at No. 8, Wouhe Inn, Jin'gang Temple Lane, Cheng Station. On the morning of the 5th, he went to the Provincial Security Corps to receive 2,500 yuan in cash, one Browning pistol, two wooden holsters, eight rifles, and fifteen bayonets. After returning to the inn for lunch, he went out to shop and had a small drink at a restaurant. He returned to the inn to rest late at 11 pm. This morning (the 6th) at 6:40 am, Li's orderly got up first, locked the room door, and told the tea boy that he was still sleeping and should not be disturbed, and that he would be back around 10 am. After finishing, he left on his own. At 11 am, the Security Corps sent someone to deliver official documents. The tea boy knocked on the door but received no response. He broke the lock and entered, seeing Li lying on the bed, with fresh blood flowing from his mouth and his tongue protruding about an inch. Lifting the quilt, he saw a hemp rope around his neck. The tea boy and others were shocked and knew that a major incident had occurred. They immediately telegraphed the Security Corps and the local Public Security Bureau to send police to the inn. Upon inspection, the 2,500 yuan in cash he had received was gone. Only 70 yuan, which his friend had entrusted to him, remained in his bag. It was clear that the orderly, Wang Qinggen, had murdered him for money by strangulation. However, no sound was heard from the next room during the murder, and how he did it is still uncertain. They immediately reported to the Hangzhou Land Court, which sent a prosecutor and officials to examine the body at 4 pm. They determined that there was only one mark from the hemp rope on the neck, and he was undoubtedly strangled to death. Afterwards, military and police agencies dispatched personnel to ports and stations to conduct strict inspections, in order to arrest the murderer and bring him to justice.

Jin'dai Bridge Car Accident 107

The No. 1035 small chartered car of the Xinshi Town Haifeng Motor Company was sending guests to Zhongshan Park in West Lake at 2 pm the day before yesterday. On the way back, it drove towards Jin'dai Bridge. A No. 104 bus of the Yonghua Company was driving towards Lingyin. The two vehicles did not honk. At that time, behind the Yonghua car, Gao Kai, a student of Huilan School and the son of Gao Yitai Cloth Store in Hangzhou, was following in a rental car. Unable to avoid it, he was knocked down by the small chartered car. The glass pieces of his glasses pierced his right eye corner and forehead, and blood flowed profusely. He was unconscious. The car took the injured person to the Municipal Hospital for treatment. Although the injuries are serious, his life is not in danger.

Old, Unemployed Man Commits Suicide by Smoking Opium 108

Zhao Hongyuan from Taizhou, over seventy years old, had been working as a Daoist at the God of Wealth Temple on Gushan Road, West Lake, for many years. Recently, he was dismissed by the temple manager for various reasons. Because of his old age and weakness, Zhao could not find a way to make a living. The night before last, he bought and consumed a large amount of opium and fell on the roadside of Gushan Road. A patrol police officer from the local sub-bureau happened to pass by and found Zhao unconscious. He was rushed to the hospital for treatment, but he died of poisoning at 8 am yesterday. Afterwards, the Hangzhou Land Court sent officials to examine the body and prepare a coffin for burial.

Rumor of Recognition of Manchukuo

Polish Envoy and American Consul Express Attitudes 109

=Wei Dentao Went to Nanjing the Night Before Last to Explain to Our Authorities=

=American Consul Said the Rumors Were Groundless=

Our reporter reports from Shanghai. A telegram from Changchun reports that the Polish envoy to Japan, Mr. Molski, went to the puppet state for inspection and made absurd remarks, saying that Poland would formally recognize Manchukuo. This has aroused the attention of our government and all parties. The Polish envoy, Mr. Wei Dentao, went to Nanjing the night before last to explain to our authorities. Also, yesterday, the American Consulate in Shanghai also denied the rumor that the United States would recognize Manchukuo. The details are as follows:

Polish Envoy Goes to Nanjing to Express Attitude 110

The Polish envoy to Japan, Mr. Molski, recently went to Manchuria for inspection and gave a speech to Japanese reporters. According to telegrams, he said that the Polish government was prepared to recognize the puppet state and planned to exchange views with the Polish consul stationed in Harbin on the specific details of recognizing the puppet state. This has aroused serious attention from all parties in China and abroad. According to a reporter from the Shenshi News Agency, in order to clarify Poland's attitude towards the puppet state, our Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently telegraphed the Polish envoy in Shanghai, asking for the truth. It is heard that the Polish envoy, Mr. Wei Dentao, in order to avoid causing ill will between China and Poland, took a night express train to Nanjing the night before last to explain to our authorities. According to another source, the remarks of the Polish envoy to Japan were based on rumors from a certain party. After receiving a telegram from the government, the Polish envoy will formally deny this statement.

American Consul Talks About Groundless Rumors 111

Also, it was recently rumored that the American government, for some reason, would change the attitude of former Secretary of State Stimson towards the recognition of Manchukuo and would have the possibility of conducting negotiations. A reporter from the Shenshi News Agency, in order to clarify the truth, went to the American Consulate to interview Consul General Mr. Cunningham. Because Mr. Cunningham was busy with official business, he was received by Consul Mr. Mewshaw. According to the conversation, regarding the rumors that the United States would recognize the puppet state, the American Consulate and Embassy had not heard anything about it. All the rumors are groundless and not credible.

Sweep Away the Evil Atmosphere and Glorify Our Han People

Mountains and Rivers as Oath, Eternal Sincerity

Zhang Zhichao, Commander-in-Chief of the National Salvation Army of Eastern China, in view of the fact that the violent Japanese instigated Pu Yi to usurp the throne and proclaim himself emperor, which has become a reality, in addition to sending his councilor Wang Chuanjing to Shanghai to report on the army's recent situation, specially issued a telegram on the Eastern Daily, asking the whole country to denounce it unanimously. Zhichao and others, by virtue of their duty, cannot but cry to our compatriots. Their deep and insidious intentions are known. First, they maneuvered in eastern Jilin, then fought bloody battles in Heilongjiang, broke Mulan, conquered Dongxing, seized warships at the mouth of the Sanpin River, and broke through heavy encirclement at the foot of the Daqing Mountains. They dispersed into parts and harassed various places. Recently, they descended on Jiamusi with a hundred riders and killed Japanese armed immigrant groups. Although they failed to restore the mountains and rivers and return our land, they can also show the patriotic spirit of our entire nation and not succumb to the oppression of the Japanese pirates. Now, the Japanese pirates are insatiable and seek to carry out further aggression, instigating the puppet Pu Yi to usurp the throne and proclaim himself emperor, intending to use the name of restoring the old power of the Qing dynasty to complete their swallowing of our entire country. It is seen that the divine and brilliant Chinese descendants will be completely annihilated by the Japanese pirates of the three islands, and the 400 million compatriots will suffer again from the remnants of despotism. All those with blood and energy cannot but be infuriated. Zhichao and others, after surviving hundreds of battles, have long placed life and death out of consideration, and are willing to be pioneers and swear to maneuver around them. The river and mountains are oath, eternal sincerity. It is hoped that compatriots across the country will rise up together to sweep away this evil atmosphere and glorify our Han people. Zhang Zhichao, Commander-in-Chief of the National Salvation Army of Eastern China, guerrilla commanders Wang Zhenqi and Wang Zhenfang, led all officers and soldiers to pay their respects to the east.

The Chinese National Products Maintenance Association Urges the Use of Domestic Silk 114

=Yesterday's Letter Suggested to the Women's National Products Movement Association=

=Do Not Buy or Manufacture Imported Artificial Silk Fabrics Again=

The Chinese National Products Maintenance Association, in order to promote the use of domestic silk, revitalize sericulture, and save the economic bankruptcy of rural areas, yesterday specially suggested to the Women's National Products Movement Committee not to buy or manufacture imported artificial silk fabrics. The original letter said, (excerpt omitted) Regarding the proposal, this year has been decided by the public as the Year of Women's National Products, and the responsibility for promoting national products should be even greater than that of men. Moreover, according to the habits of our Chinese families, men manage outside and women manage inside. All the necessities of a family, such as clothing, food, entertainment, etc., are handled by the hostess, and the master does not ask about it. If the hostess can adhere to the principle of not using anything but national products and insist on implementing it, then

Foreign Goods Will Be Eliminated 115

It can be expected in a matter of days, and national wealth and strength can be assured. Our association has been committed to promoting national products and revitalizing industries for more than 20 years. As for the results, where are the results? With an import surplus of 900 million, the country is on the verge of bankruptcy. Saving the dying is too late, and it is extremely heartbreaking. I have examined the reason, which is the lack of strength and no way to punish. Empty words are useless and are forgotten in a blink of an eye. Those in power cannot set an example themselves, practice diligently, and save the unprecedented disaster. To Wash Away This Shame 116

To revitalize the national spirit of our great Chinese nation. It is found that in recent years, the bankruptcy of rural areas in our country has become increasingly serious, and it is urgent to find ways to save it. Otherwise, if the skin does not exist, what will the fur adhere to? However, if we want to save it, we must first revitalize sericulture, and to revitalize sericulture, it is especially necessary to promote the use of domestic silk fabrics. Because our silk has been a famous national quintessence for thousands of years. Since the import and sale of foreign silk satin, wool, and artificial silk fabrics into China, our silk industry has been squeezed, declining year by year. Today, it is in a dying state, with a tendency to disappear completely. Seven or eight out of ten silk factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have closed down. If we talk about saving rural areas in this way, is it not going south by driving the chariot north? I suggest that the following two things be resolved, widely publicized, announced to the country, and earnestly implemented in order to reverse the decline and consolidate the foundation of the country. (1) Strictly prohibit wearing Europeanized imported clothes such as overcoats. (2) Do not buy or manufacture imported artificial silk fabrics again. The two items on the right are the fundamental plan for promoting domestic silk, revitalizing sericulture, and saving rural areas. Because the prosperity of domestic silk will naturally lead to the prosperity of sericulture, and the prosperity of sericulture will lead to the prosperity of the rural economy. This is a natural principle and they are interconnected. This matter is of great importance, and it is hoped that the public will decide to implement it.

Seamen's Union Advocates Recovering Inland Waterway Navigation Rights 117

The Preparatory Committee of the Chinese Seamen's Union Telegraphed: All provincial and municipal party departments, governments at all levels, legal entities, and newspapers for your perusal.

In independent countries around the world, the navigation of inland rivers is prohibited to foreign vessels, in order to protect the domestic shipping industry. Since our country signed unequal treaties in the late Qing Dynasty, inland waterway navigation rights have fallen into the hands of foreigners. As a result, foreign vessels can freely travel in our mainland, seize the market, and manipulate commerce, causing the shipping industry run by Chinese people to be greatly affected and losing its development space, forming today's economic decline. Speaking of this, it is unbearable to be sad and indignant. Now that the Sino-British and Sino-American commercial shipping treaties have expired, we should take the opportunity to recover inland waterway navigation rights and abolish the previous unequal treaties. In addition to submitting a request to the Ministry of Communications to send representatives to participate in the shipping conference in order to contribute opinions, our association also hopes that the people of the country will work together with one heart, advocate unanimously, and urge the government to negotiate strictly to achieve the goal of recovery, in order to save the doom of our country's shipping industry. The future of the country depends on it. A special telegram is sent for your information, which is extremely urgent. The Preparatory Committee of the Chinese Seamen's Union kowtows, fish.

Telegram Requesting Transfer of Order to Guangdong and Fujian Provinces to Collect Import Tax on Foreign Rice 118

Last year, the China Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau wanted to seek control of agricultural products to prevent the encroachment of foreign rice, and the government also successively relaxed the ban on grain exports and increased the import tax on foreign rice and wheat. These are all good policies to relieve people's livelihood. However, the order for the tax on foreign rice and wheat is exclusive to Guangdong, Fujian, and Guangxi provinces. The government's intention is to expect that the Guangdong and Fujian provinces have already established bureaus by the provincial government to collect taxes separately, in order to avoid duplication, and temporarily exclude them. As for the people's food in Guangxi province, it can be self-sufficient. Since there is no need to rely on foreign rice, there is no need to increase the tax. However, Guangdong and Fujian provinces have always been areas short of rice. Before the new tax was announced, they were purchased in Shanghai, Hunan, and Anhui areas. After the announcement, they stopped. The tax rate has not been unified, and foreign rice takes the opportunity to dump. Although Guangdong and Fujian provinces have separately established bureaus to collect taxes, the tax rate is only one-third of the customs duty. This is tantamount to opening one side of the net in South China and giving foreign rice an opportunity to invade. According to statistics, since the middle of last month, 400,000 bags of foreign rice have been imported into Guangdong province from Hong Kong, and they are still following each other. Fujian province also has a huge amount. American aviator

Economic Commission Sends Personnel to Inspect Lianghuai Salt Area Again 120

According to Reports, There are 13 Million Mu of Wasteland

If Converted to Cotton Fields, 3 Million Dan Can Be Collected Annually

The National Economic Commission, in order to investigate the area of wasteland in the Lianghuai salt area and prepare for reclamation, specially organized an inspection team to the Lianghuai salt area to conduct on-site inspections. It is learned that the inspection team has completed the inspection and reported the results to the Economic Commission. It is said that there are a total of 13 million mu of wasteland in Lianghuai. If all of them are opened up for planting cotton, it can produce one dan of clean cotton for every four mu, and can collect 3 million dan of net cotton every year, which is enough to resist the total amount of imported cotton. However, in order to be prudent, the Economic Commission plans to select experts for a second inspection to conduct a detailed survey of the soil, water conservancy basic projects, and what kind of cotton varieties are suitable for planting. Once this second inspection is completed, it will begin to reclaim the land.

Effective Yesterday at Ten Percent

The state-owned China Merchants Bureau, along with the privately-owned San Bei, Ningshao, British Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and Japanese Nisshin shipping companies, a total of six, had previously, due to the shallow waters of the Yangtze River and the danger of heavily laden ships navigating, increased the Shanghai to Hankou freight rate by 25% as a shallow water surcharge starting on January 25th. Now, due to the gradual rise of the river water level, a joint meeting of the six companies in Shanghai decided to reduce the shallow water surcharge from Shanghai to Hankou to 10% starting yesterday. Yesterday, all shipping companies have complied and implemented this decision.
