Education News - Out of Town

Jiangsu Province's County Supervisors Begin Mutual Inspection and Guidance 203

Granted Emergency Powers

(Wuxi Dispatch) In order to strictly rectify education and improve efficiency, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education has implemented mutual inspection and guidance among county supervisors in each county, and granted county supervisors emergency powers. The ten counties of Xishan, Wuxi, Yushan, Yixing, Licheng, Jingjiang, Jintan, Wuxian, and Wujiang form the Second Normal School District. The Provincial Department of Education has separately stipulated the mutual inspection and guidance of supervisors. Yesterday, the "Joint Meeting of the Second Normal School District's Zonal Inspection and Guidance and the Second Normal School District's Primary School Education Research Association" was held in the Wuxi Provincial Normal School conference room. More than twenty people attended, including county supervisors from the ten counties such as Sun Youguang, Xu Wenlan, Pan Jishan, and Shen Xanzhi. The chairman was Shen Peixian. Many important proposals were passed. Regarding the emergency treatment measures, it was also discussed and decided to have Song Yunsun draft a form to be submitted to the Provincial Department for reporting, so that it can be applied. As for the three supervisors who were transferred to Wuxi for inspection and guidance, Xu Zaofei from Qingpu, Hu Chaolun from Jiangyin, and Xu Shaolie from Kunshan, have already arrived in Wuxi. The two county supervisors from this county who were transferred to Wuxian for inspection and guidance, Song Yunsun and Shen Xanzhi, are scheduled to depart today. This mutual inspection and guidance is scheduled to end on June 15th. Another inspection and guidance meeting will be held on July 5th to discuss all the reforms and improvements in the education of each county after the mutual inspection and guidance.

Ministry of Education Inspectors of Higher Education Inspecting in Jinan 204

The Ministry of Education previously sent inspectors to inspect higher education in Jinan, Tianjin, Beiping, Baoding, Kaifeng, Wuhan, Changsha, and Anqing. Except for Zhou Tianfang, who is waiting in Beiping for all the members to arrive and inspect together, and Hao Gengsheng, who will participate in the Ministry of Education's Sports Committee on the 14th and rush to Beiping on the 15th and 16th to join the inspection, the remaining members are waiting for the Ministry of Education to designate someone to inspect medicine before departing together. The Ministry of Education issued an order on the 5th to appoint Pang Jingzhou to inspect medical education together with the members, and the Secretariat sent letters on the 5th to specialized schools or education bureaus above the specialized level in Jinan, Tianjin, Beiping, Baoding, Kaifeng, Wuhan, Changsha, and Anqing, explaining that the Ministry of Education had sent the members to inspect and asking them to investigate. It is said that Chen Kezhong, Guo Youshou, Sun Guofeng, Liu Yingshi, Pang Jingzhou, etc., left Pukou by train for Jinan on the morning of the 6th. The members are scheduled to start inspecting in Jinan today (7th). This inspection will cover all schools above the specialized level, whether public or private, and whether or not they have been registered. There are especially many schools in Beiping, about twenty schools. According to the Ministry of Education's deadline, it is limited to one month and a few days, but in reality, in order to achieve comprehensive and serious inspection, the deadline may need to be slightly extended.

A Glimpse of the Shandong Provincial Education Inspection Report 205

Report by Ministry of Education Specialist Guo Youshou

Ministry of Education specialist Guo Youshou previously inspected Shandong Province's education and has now prepared a report and submitted it to the Ministry of Education. The original report is divided into twelve chapters (1. Introduction, 2. Educational Administration, 3. Educational Funding, 4. Kindergarten Education, 5. Primary School Education, 6. Secondary School Education, 7. Normal School Education, 8. Vocational Education, 9. Social Education, 10. Zouping County Education, 11. Recommendations, 12. Appendix). The text is very long. Here is an excerpt from the introduction, which can also give a glimpse of Shandong Province's education. The introduction roughly states that in 1928, Shandong underwent a major change in the course of history. The tide of the National Revolution, along with the National Revolutionary Army, arrived in Shandong, and the reform of all social undertakings began, especially the most significant changes in education. Since its establishment, the Department of Education has lasted for five and a half years. In the first year, Jinan and Jiaodong were still in the hands of the Japanese, and the northwest was filled with bandits. The provincial government was entrenched in Tai'an. In order to establish a foundation for party-state education, the Department of Education strived to restore the damaged school buildings and gather the scattered students, and the regulations were organized and innovated, roughly forming a rudimentary framework. Around April of 1930, Shandong suffered war again, and the provincial government moved east to Qingdao. The education of all counties in the province returned to the path of destruction. The foundation of two years of effort was suddenly interrupted. After the recovery of Jinan, reconstruction was restarted. In the past three years, considerable results have been achieved in the continued fundraising and auditing of provincial and county education funds (in 1933, the provincial education fund was 3,031,399 yuan, an increase of 112,534 yuan compared to the previous year. Each year from 1930 to 1931 gradually increased. In 1933, the county education funds, excluding Heze and Zouping counties, which have been changed to experimental counties (Zouping 86,626 yuan last year, Heze 193,009 yuan), the remaining 106 counties totaled 4,364,339 yuan in annual education funds. Shandong's education funds were extremely chaotic before 1928. After the establishment of the Department of Education, active rectification was carried out and open methods were adopted. In the past five or six years, the results have been remarkable. Education funds have maintained their independence. Other matters, such as formulating a unified system, clearing up assets, and auditing and supervising, are too numerous to mention, sweeping away the old bad habits. Schools are no longer regarded as sources of profit, and the management of education funds has entered a normal track), the establishment of provincial and county rural normal schools, the overall planning of the establishment of middle schools, the promotion of compulsory education, and the improvement of social education have all achieved considerable results. Youshou was dispatched to Shandong in October 1933 to inspect, which lasted for a month, passing through Jinan City, and 14 counties including Taian, Qufu, Ziyang, Jining, Qihe, Pingyuan, Dexian, Zhangqiu, Zouping, Changshan, Yidu, Linzi, Huangxian, and Fushan. Among the provincial schools, I inspected eight middle schools, four normal schools, three rural normal schools and vocational schools each, three provincial social education institutions, and also inspected eight private middle schools, four county middle schools, one rural normal school, four normal school training institutes, three vocational supplementary schools, about 60 provincial, municipal/district, and private primary schools and kindergartens, and more than ten local education administration and social education institutions (omitted below).

Anhui Education Director Yang Lian Suddenly Suffers Facial Paralysis 206

Anhui Education Director Yang Lian recently requested a ten-day leave from the provincial government, and took a ship to Beijing on the afternoon of the 2nd, in a hurry, saying that he had important official business to report to the Ministry. According to reliable information, Yang's trip to Beijing was due to a sudden onset of a strange disease where his mouth was slanted to the left, so he went to Beijing for medical treatment. It is said that Yang had been working too hard in Anhui, and often took walks in the suburbs during his free time. A few days ago, he was accidentally blown by a strong wind, which suddenly caused his mouth to slant to the left. There were no famous doctors in Anhui, so he requested leave to go to Beijing to consult the Central Hospital. It is said that this disease is very strange and may not be able to recover for a while. Although Yang's mouth is crooked, his spirit is still normal.

Following the Oriental Library, the Hongying Library is Actively Preparing 210

Plans to Open for Trial Operation This Autumn Before the New Building is Constructed

Selecting Historical Materials, Currently Has One Million Items, 40,000 Books

Social Sciences, Especially History, is the Core of the Library

After the Site is Decided, a Public Library Will Also Be Attached

Since the outbreak of the Songhu War, China's greatest Oriental Library was destroyed, and people at home and abroad have expressed regret. Now, industrialist Ye Hongying has donated a large sum of money to accept the Humanities Library, which was being prepared by the Humanities Society, and established the Hongying Library. Its scale cannot be compared with the Oriental Library, but it focuses on selecting historical materials and collecting a vast amount of resources, which is unprecedented in Shanghai. The preparation process and implementation plan are described below:

Source of the Library's Name - The Hongying Library is receiving the Humanities Library of the Humanities Society. The Humanities Society was formerly known as the Jiazi Society. It was initiated and organized by Huang Renzhi, Ma Junqing, Shi Liangcai, and others in July 1924. Part of its work was dedicated to selecting historical materials, called "Humanities Series." In March 1925, it established a location on Jing'an Temple Road and began work. Funding was donated independently by Ma Junqing. In 1927 and 1928, the scope was temporarily reduced. In March 1929, with the help of Qian Xinzhi and Xu Jingren, the plan was revived. In addition to historical materials, it also engaged in compiling magazine indexes, publishing monthly magazines and series, and preparing for the Humanities Library. In March 1931, the society's sixth annual meeting resolved to officially name it the Humanities Society and elected Qian Xinzhi and others as standing committee members. In 1932, it planned to build a library building. According to the resolution of the seventh annual meeting, the budget for land purchase and construction fees and funds was 400,000 yuan, and it was stipulated that if a private individual made an independent donation, the library would be named after that person. Ye Hongying happened to visit the society and deeply approved of it. Subsequently, the Hongying Education Fund was initiated, donating 500,000 yuan in cash. After deducting 100,000 yuan for the rural primary school fund, 400,000 yuan was specifically used for the library fund. The board of directors of the fund resolved that on April 3, 1933, Ye Hongying, Cai Yuanpei, Qian Xinzhi, Shen Enfu, Huang Yanpei, and others exchanged documents, and on June 7, personnel were dispatched to take inventory, and the name was changed to Hongying Library.

Library Construction Plan - The library focuses on social sciences, with history as the core of social sciences. It first collects as much as possible about modern history and its historical materials. The preparation office is currently located on Avenue Joffre...

Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education Announces Publicly Funded Overseas Study Examination 211

A total of five positions; examination on April 3rd.

The following is the outline of the Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education's announcement of the examination for publicly funded overseas study in Europe and America: 1. Number of positions: five (the number will be doubled for the preliminary examination); 2. Countries of study and selected departments: Germany or the United States, two positions in engineering (electrical engineering, mechanical engineering, civil engineering), one selected from these three departments; chemical engineering (papermaking), one position; United Kingdom or the United States, business administration, one position; Germany, veterinary medicine, one position; France or the United States, agronomic chemistry, one position; 3. Qualifications for Examination: Any person who is registered as a resident of Jiangxi and possesses one of the following qualifications, and whose examination is confirmed, may take the examination: (1) Graduates of public or registered private specialized schools or above, at home or abroad, who have held technical positions related to their field of study for more than one year; (2) Graduates of public or registered private specialized schools or above, at home or abroad, who have continued to study their field of study for more than two years and have valuable works or other achievements; (3) Graduates of public or registered private universities or independent colleges at home or abroad with excellent grades; 4. Registration Procedures: When registering, in addition to submitting a graduation certificate and two recent four-inch half-length photos, and a registration fee of two yuan, those who meet the qualifications in the first clause of the preceding article must also submit two copies each of their resume and employment certificate; those who meet the qualifications in the second clause of the preceding article must also submit specialized works or other achievements; those who meet the qualifications in the third clause of the preceding article must also submit a grade transcript, employment certificate, or school grade transcript. The service certificate or school transcript must be signed and sealed by the head of the school or the school principal; 5. Registration Date and Location: From March 1st to 31st, 1934, register at the Jiangxi Department of Education; 6. Examination Subjects, Location, and Time: (1) Preliminary Examination: A. Physical Examination: 9:00 AM to 4:00 PM on April 5th at the Provincial Medical College. Those who fail the physical examination will not be allowed to take the examination; B. Written Examination: Held at the Jiangxi Department of Education; (1) General Subjects; (2) Specialized Subjects; (2) Re-examination: Held at the Ministry of Education from July 1st to 15th; 7. Calculation of Examination Results: Party Principles, Chinese Language, and National History and Geography in the general subjects account for 25% of the total score; the language of the country of study accounts for 25%; specialized subjects account for 50%; 8. Standards for Publicly Funded Students.

It is proposed that half of the funds be used for the construction of a library and equipment, with the address proposed to be in the western section of the French Concession or near Hongqiao Road, which has not yet been determined. After the location of the library is decided, a public library will be established in the nearby area, dedicated to the public for reading. It is now decided by the preparatory office to open the library for trial operation at the current location before the new building is constructed, which is expected to be around the turn of summer and autumn. The office is divided into four departments: administrative affairs, historical materials, publishing, and library & indexing. The selected historical materials, from the Xinhai Revolution to the present day, total 939,824 items; books and magazines total 42,200 volumes; charts and diagrams, 155 pieces; and abstracts index of magazines and newspapers, 100,9682 items.

Trial Opening Method: Since the Preparatory Office of the Hongying Library moved to the newly rented house on Xiafei Road, the house has a lawn in front, with fresh air and a quiet environment, suitable for reading. On the one hand, land is being purchased and constructed in an orderly manner, and on the other hand, it is planned to open for trial operation first to meet the public's expectations. The methods are as follows: (1) Six or eight temporary houses in the style of barracks will be built on the west side of the lawn, and the books, magazines, and historical materials on the lower floor will be moved into them successively, vacating the lower floor houses for open reading of books. These temporary houses can be dismantled and moved for use after the new building is completed; (2) After the temporary houses are built, the historical materials will be moved first, vacating half a room for use. When there are gradually more readers, the books and magazines will be moved into the temporary houses together for full use; (3) The opening method adopts a limited opening. Those who want to read books must first obtain a book reading certificate according to the corresponding procedures. The procedures and format of the book reading certificate will be determined separately; (4) The historical materials are being sorted out. At this time, work is being stepped up. It is necessary to wait until the review and editing are completed and the materials are bound before they can be opened with extremely careful procedures. It is not convenient to open them for public reading at this time, but with the introduction of people related to this office, those who request to read them through special procedures as usual are not subject to this rule; (5) The existing books and magazines, including donations, total more than 42,000 volumes as of the end of January. There are quite a few magazines among them, and most of the books are biased towards general knowledge, which is still not enough for practical application. It is found that the original plan for the library, which had been approved, stipulated a book purchase fee of 30,000 yuan. If it is decided to open at this time, the quantity should be specified, and the scope should still be in accordance with the approved plan, with social sciences as the scope and the history category in social sciences as the core. Detailed methods for purchasing books will be determined separately; (6) The opening time should be based on the completion of the sorting out of the existing books. After this method is approved, work should be accelerated, which will probably have to wait until summer or early autumn before it can be opened. Additional personnel will be added to prepare for the opening, and temporary expenses will be increased. The budget will be determined separately.

Rules for Donating Books: The rules for donating books and documents to the office are as follows: (1) All those who sympathize with this office and are willing to donate books or documents will be handled by this office in accordance with the rules; (2) All books or documents that are reviewed to have historical material properties and do not violate the following items will be gladly preserved by this office: A. Those that meet the needs of this office; B. Those that are suitable for preservation by this office; (3) After receiving the donated books and documents, this office will issue a receipt to the donor for safekeeping; (4) The donor may apply to this office for the recovery of the donated books and documents as needed, and return the receipt. This office may also terminate the donation as needed or deem it unsuitable for preservation, and apply to the donor for the recovery and return of the receipt; (5) This office shall do its best to protect the donated books and documents, but this does not apply to irresistible facts such as natural disasters and man-made disasters; (6) For those who donate books or documents, this office will send a letter of thanks and give a publication to the donor as appropriate. They may also come to this office to request to inspect books or archives as needed, in order to reward their kindness.

Various Academic Groups' Collection Team to Hainan Arrives on Qiong Island 212

The customs of the abandoned lunar New Year are unique and far from the Central Plains

Excellent materials obtained in the field of anthropology

The Hainan Biological Science Collection Team, organized by the Jing Sheng Biological Survey Institute of Peiping, the Museum of Natural History of the Academia Sinica, the Biological Research Institute of the Science Society of China, and Shandong University, Peking University, etc., departed from Shanghai in mid-January and then met with the Guangdong Geological Survey Institute in Guangzhou, and went to Hainan together. They arrived safely on Qiong Island at the beginning of last month. According to the person in charge of the Biological Research Institute of the Science Society of China, who spoke to a Shanghai reporter, a letter was recently received from Mr. Wang Yikang, the captain of the sea team of the team, stating that the land team arrived in Yansheng on February 7. Yansheng is located on the southern foot of Wuzhi Mountain, in the very center of Qiong Island, and is an important place on Qiong Island. After the abandoned lunar New Year's Day, they immediately engaged in the investigation of land products. Because Qiong Island is located in a remote part of Hainan, adheres to old customs, and attaches great importance to celebrating the abandoned lunar New Year, all projects are suspended, so it is impossible to work immediately. However, excellent materials were obtained in the field of anthropological research at this time. The customs of the abandoned lunar New Year are unique and far from the North and South of the Yangtze River. The Institute of History and Philology of the Academia Sinica has also recently allocated 500 yuan to assist the investigation in the field of anthropology. The sea team is stationed in Haikou and also needs to wait until after the abandoned lunar New Year's Day before it can carry out hunting. Generally, they have been working hard for the past month. Mr. Wang's letter also stated that the team's mailing address is Hainan Bookstore, Bo'ai Road, Haikou, Qiongzhou. Those who want to inquire about them from the outside can directly send letters to that address.

Biological Research Institute of the Science Society of China Pays Attention to the Investigation of Native Products 213

Jiangxi Provincial Government Economic Commission sends a letter requesting clarification on fish species

The Biological Society of Beijing Middle Schools plans to hold public lectures

The Biological Research Institute of the Science Society of China in Nanjing has been established for ten years. All staff members of the institute are Chinese, and they have been studying diligently and have achieved outstanding results. More than 100 of their published papers have attracted considerable attention from foreign academic institutions. However, they have never engaged in publicity, so people in China are not very aware of them. Since the institute held a public exhibition last month, visitors have been amazed by their efforts. The institute's work pays the most attention to the investigation of native products, but it is constrained by financial resources and cannot be developed to the fullest extent. The construction departments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces often have troubles, and they often use the fact that there are not many personnel to avoid sharing their time and effort to serve the provinces. Recently, the Economic Commission of the Jiangxi Provincial Government sent an official letter to them, requesting them to clarify the types of fish in Jiangxi and their producing areas. The institute has already sent a reply, and sent several publications, stating that although the fish species in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River have been slightly investigated, due to the lack of financial and human resources, they have not been able to conduct a detailed investigation. What is known about Jiangxi Province is even less. If convenience can be provided in the future, specialists will be sent to conduct a detailed investigation. It is also heard that the Biology Teaching and Research Association of Nanjing Middle Schools plans to invite researchers from the institute to hold regular public lectures, which has been accepted, and the schedule is currently being planned, and it will be implemented soon.

(Omission) In order to take care of the friendship between the two sides, we dare not give advice. Directory of Graduates of Nango, Dongda, and Zhongda Published 222

The General Association of Graduates of National Nango, Dongda, and Zhongda published a directory of members in 1931, which only included the names of the members who had joined the association. It felt that it was not enough for application. Now, in order to promote communication, the association has compiled and printed a directory of graduates, which includes all graduates of all official departments of Nango, Dongda, and Zhongda in the past, whether they have joined the association or not. The investigation and verification took a long time. It has recently been published and is divided into three parts, from the first class of graduates of Nango in 1917 to the sixth class of graduates of Zhongda in 1933. The names, nicknames, native places, service institutions, and contact addresses are all recorded in detail. The binding is exquisite, and it is easy to carry. It also has accurate statistics on the number of graduates in each period. All members who have joined the association and paid the membership fee will be given a copy. Those who have not joined the association or have not paid the full membership fee must first go to the association to complete the membership registration and pay the full or supplementary membership fee before they can receive a copy.

Free Talk

On Suicide 224

— Wu Biyan

"The best fruits are often the first to rot!" Excellent young people often fail to achieve anything, and clever children are difficult to raise to adulthood - this is probably true based on human experience.

In modern times, many young people commit suicide. What are the reasons? Economic oppression, failed love, or seeing through the world of mortals… What are the methods? Several suicide notes, or taking poison, or throwing oneself into the river, or lying on the railway tracks… What are the results? Rescued, or really died!

People who are deliberately forced to death do not count. Those who commit suicide voluntarily are truly lamentable! Broadly speaking, those who are alive may not be happy to die, so it is still mostly due to the environment that forces them to die, and perhaps mostly intentional. Many old people spare no effort to inflict fatal injuries on the new youth simply because they cannot get used to them or feel that they are in the way. The elimination of many young people under the age of twenty in the past seven or eight years is clear evidence. What's more, there were female students bleeding to death in front of the Beijing government. Then these responsibilities have those who bear them. There has always been "a wrong has a head, and a debt has an owner." If people are forced to death, they may receive retribution on themselves or their children and grandchildren. Cause and effect are never false, especially in matters of life and death, which are believable.

The remaining causes of suicide are few. The orchid burns itself to give light, the ointment consumes itself to give light, rushing around, without a moment of peace, ending with an unresolved end, like Wang Guowei, then the reason is that he lost "too much truth," and took life too seriously! Or after a setback or repeated setbacks, all thoughts are ashes, and the spirit entrusted to it dies first, then the remaining shell of the body is regarded as not worth cherishing, and death is regarded as returning home. The reason is that it lost "too much fragility," like Ai Xia, unable to withstand wind and rain, like tender spring flowers. Many spring flower-like children have withered like this.

In the vast sea of people, the feelings of life and death are endlessly connected, and the suicide of a few young people is truly like losing a hair from nine oxen. But for the future of the entire society, it is clearly a sign, which shows that Chinese youth share the joys and sorrows of the world and also suffer from the era's diseases, feeling pain and wandering. Although it is decadent, it is already an expression of strength, just as women who are poisoned by "wallpaper" must have pain and a future birth, although we do not know at all what the trends of this era and what will be produced in the future.

He Jiahuai's Creative Problems 225

— Shi Heng

The day before yesterday, I saw Mr. He Jiahuai's "About My Creation" article in this publication. The article was well written; however, the facts it provides still need to be discussed. The scavenger article that Mr. He mentioned was published in the recent "Culture Train"; the scavenger does indeed have another identity. Although I know it, I am not convenient to announce it here. If necessary or even in legal trouble, someone will be responsible. The scavenger is a pseudonym of my friend, but the news he released was originally heard from my mouth, so I can't help but be responsible for this matter. It is not to defend the scavenger, but now that things have come to this point, I have to make the facts I know public.

Mr. He and I have never known each other, so it is understandable that there is no grievance or hatred. I have no intention of antagonizing Mr. He at all, and now I have no choice but to come forward.

I first heard about the suspicion of Mr. He's creation last summer in Nanjing on a certain evening near Houhu. The speaker was Chu Anping (a friend of both Mr. He and Mr. Xu); besides me, Gao Zhi was also listening. Anping said: "He Jiahuai and Xu Zhuanpeng's novels are unclear. Sometimes the original manuscript is written with Xu Zhuanpeng's name, but the published magazine changes it to He Jiahuai." He gave an example of the title at the time, but unfortunately I forgot. Because it was just idle talk, I didn't pay much attention to it, and I hadn't met Zhuanpeng at that time, so the matter passed.

Later, as I became more familiar with Zhuanpeng, I occasionally talked about this matter. At first, Zhuanpeng denied it, but from the expression in his reply, it could be seen that he was pretending. After asking more questions, he finally admitted it. Originally, it was just a joke out of curiosity, but after it was proven to be true, I felt very uncomfortable in my heart. I was not only dissatisfied with Mr. He, but also very unhappy with Zhuanpeng, because although there are many scandals in the Shanghai literary world, such things are rare.

"How many articles are there in total?" I asked Zhuanpeng.

"Probably about ten, you could say it's all my works from 1932," Zhuanpeng replied.

This proves even more that the fault is not entirely on Mr. He alone. If it is one or two articles, it is understandable out of friendship. But if there are as many as ten, it is too outrageous. At that time, I scolded Zhuanpeng unceremoniously and asked him not to ask for this kind of thing again in the future. (However, Zhuanpeng has another explanation, describing the whole story, but I am not convenient to disclose it now without Zhuanpeng's permission.)

"Then how did Anping know about this?" I asked.

"This matter is probably not known to Anping alone," Zhuanpeng said. "I'm afraid Shen Congwen, Shi Zhecun, and Shao Xunmei all know about it, because I gave one of my articles to Congwen to revise first, and he revised a lot, but when it was published, it became He Jiahuai's name; often articles were first submitted to "Modern" and "New Moon," written with my name, but after being taken back and published in other magazines, the name was changed again."

But Zhuanpeng's guess was wrong, because the editors couldn't pay that much attention. When I had the chance to ask Zhecun, he said he didn't know.

I have to take responsibility. This news was inadvertently told by me, and the scavenger's article came from this.

In me, there is no intention to make enemies with Mr. He, and Mr. He is still a new writer. If I announced it as if it were a big deal, I was afraid it would be detrimental to Mr. He, so I once told Zhuanpeng to clear up this matter secretly, return the things to their original owner, and then no one would speak again. Zhuanpeng was also quite eager to get the articles back, encouraged by his friends, but he was finally too embarrassed to deal with Mr. He directly, only saying that he would slowly think of a way. Recently, he returned to his hometown and wrote me a letter, pointing out Du Heng, Zhecun, Cunren and I to handle this matter on his behalf, and said that on his side, I have "full authority", which is really a difficult problem. Please think, how can this kind of pro bono lawyer do it!

Together with Cunren, I ran to the Modern Bookstore and talked with Du Heng and Zhecun. The result of the discussion was that the publication of Mr. He's collection of creations "Rainy Day," which was being printed at the Modern Bookstore, was temporarily suspended, and Zhuanpeng was asked to write a letter to Modern, clearly listing his own works and extracting them. However, it has been half a month since this resolution was notified to Zhuanpeng, and his letter has not yet arrived. Probably this public figure is hesitating again. Then, if I, the pro bono lawyer with "full authority," loses the plaintiff as well, and becomes a legal person myself, how can this lawsuit be fought? Now Mr. He himself has come forward to ask people, implicating a scavenger, and I have to provide the whole story as above.

As for Mr. He's explanation of his creation in the article "About My Creation," I think it's a bit of bragging; his so-called (1) tight layout, (2) detailed description, (3) very careful use of words and sentences, are very appropriate criticisms of Zhuanpeng's novels, which he himself does not have at all. Mr. He is too thick-skinned. Among the masterpieces he considers satisfactory, such as "Drawing Water" and "Release from Prison," it is clear that they are Zhuanpeng's works. Does this still require critics to come forward to research and analyze them? Fortunately, the original manuscripts of Zhuanpeng's creations are all preserved, and they can be printed out when necessary.

But we always hope that Mr. He can bravely admit his mistakes, return the things to their original owner, and work hard from now on, or there will still be infinite hope for the future; otherwise, if he only cares about the present and argues arbitrarily, and the matter is therefore publicized, then he will be even more despised.

Random Notes (Continued) 226

— Xia Chang

(Nine)

I have repeatedly mentioned courtesy articles such as epitaphs. Recently, I read an article by Qiao Bo, satirizing epitaphs, and the language is extremely humorous. Its meaning is: "When writing epitaphs for people, the seeker will not be satisfied if the deeds are not filled in; the viewer will not believe it if the deeds are filled in too much. When there is nothing to say, I have no choice but to copy excerpts and various editions to respond. It's like taking a portrait from the face of a dead person, which is not enough to resemble, let alone writing the appearance of a passerby? I hope that people in the world will do some good deeds and be good people before they die, so that those who write epitaphs will hesitate to write and cover up for them." Making people for the sake of the glory of the epitaph, this kind of satire can be said to be wishful thinking.

(Ten)

Today's authors mostly write creative experiences, and there are not many good ones among them. Most of them praise themselves, and some even take it as an honor to ask others to write such articles, thinking that it is a good opportunity to show off. I really dare not praise a word. Xu Rijiuyun: "I still remember twenty years ago, when I was extremely distressed, unable to live or die, writing all day, worrying all day, and living all day. I didn't dare to show the article to others, and my face turned red when I showed it to others, thinking that it was unbearable to be trivialized, and it was also unbearable to be praised. Or, unfortunately, to be caught by those who talk about exaggeration, it is even more unbearable. But today's speakers and writers in the world do not first measure their abilities, and externally measure the lovableness of others, deceive their hearts and create karma, and praise their predecessors, but in fact, they don't even know that they have fallen into the ghost country, which is also pitiful." Like this kind of frank spirit and angry accusation, I really don't know how many times I have seen it in our writers' self-reports, although there are also such people.

(Ten)(One)

Someone is named Huang Huanghe, and Zhou Baian humorously joked with him: "The Yellow Crane Tower is named after the immortal picking orange peel into a crane and dancing. The Yellow Crane Peak is named after the peak being full of pine flowers and the crane's back being yellow. Sir, are you made of orange peel, or are you covered with pine flowers? One of the two is too empty. I'm afraid that the empty hunger will kill the gentleman who wants to get on the crane's back." The language is quite interesting.

The Night Before Leaving Home 227

— Li Qiao

Stepping into the room, my wife looked at me silently, as if there was something to say, but couldn't say it for a while.

I couldn't help but be silent.

After a while, my wife lowered her head, and then raised her head to look at me again:

"Have you packed your things?"

"Um."

"Is there anything else you want?"

"No."

I replied slowly, looking at my wife's face: extremely sad! She sat on the edge of the bed, her dark eyes always reluctantly looking at me. This made me feel the pain of parting too!

I lowered my head, wanting to say something to comfort her. However, I couldn't say a word! The room was silent and a little desolate.

After a while, my wife asked me with a choked voice: "After you leave tomorrow, when will you be able to come back?..."

"I can come back anytime." I suppressed the sadness in my heart and joked with my wife as usual.

My wife barely forced a bitter smile:

"Really come back any day? You don't think about how sad I am when you are outside! You are so cruel!"

I deliberately teased my wife:

"I go out to help people... I have to suffer people's anger and be scolded by people. That's what's sad! What's sad about you at home?"

My wife looked bitter and sighed a long sigh:

"Who knows my suffering?... Alas, I really don't like to be separated from you often, but what can I do? After you leave, I'm all alone, having to manage the house and busy with the work in the vegetable garden, think about it...!" "Then, I won't go out, I'll stay home with you, okay?"

"No, you have to go out!" My wife glanced at me: "However, don't be like you were in previous years, coming home with a mess of debt. The family still owes people money, and I still owe Third Sister a stone of grain!"

Listening to my wife's words, I silently faced the half-bright and half-dim dying lamp, and I was just thinking in my heart: How can I not come home with a mess of debt?

Without my noticing, my wife secretly shed tears!

No Snow (5) 229

— Miao Chongqun

Although there are hundreds of thousands of generals commanding the army on the front line, they have become frightened birds, with no contact at all. The lifeline of transportation has been completely cut off. The front line is empty. The front line only has hundreds of thousands of meat-made bullets.

Therefore, the cars, carriages, rickshaws, pushcarts, water carts, ox carts... even people and camels in the city were requisitioned overnight, and they were loaded with pancakes, dry steamed buns, artillery shells, and bullets... and set off to the front line together. This long transport team composed of civilians, carriages, water carts, and camels, viewed from above from a high altitude, may gradually form a "丁" shape with the Great Wall of the north. The top stroke of the "丁" was built with the fat and bones of the people thousands of years ago. Now, the bottom stroke of the "丁" is driving thousands of lives to pile up. We don't know when the violent aggressors will disappear or never disappear, but this Great Wall, no matter what it is built of, has permanently become a tragic and generous record in the history of our nation. It may one day be taken away from the increasingly decadent and weak by the violent aggressor, but the bricks and stones on the city, which have been stained and soaked with the blood, sweat and spirit of our ancestors, its glory will forever shine in this world.

On the first day of the departure of the civilian and camel transport team, they saw earthen houses and withered trees. On the second day, they saw collapsed houses and burnt trees. On the third day, they saw dead mules and horses and human corpses. On the road, there was white snow left over from winter that had not yet melted, and it was also mixed with the bright red blood of people that seemed to have just flowed out... It had already frozen into pieces... The winding Great Wall was right in front of them. Over there, the daytime was covered with pitch-black smoke, and the night was filled with blood-like flames. The enemy's planes, like flocks of mountain birds, circled around the horizon, sometimes high, sometimes low, sometimes near, sometimes far. The sound was extremely deafening. With the sound of the planes, countless black dots fell down. Each black dot was a bomb weighing more than two hundred pounds. The booming sound, the bursting sound, the wasteland became its broadcasting field, and the valley became a very accurate echo machine.

Pieces of clothing, pieces of stone, pieces of meat... immediately burst and flew up, and turned into countless and countless small black dots. The coming of these black dots, the going of those black dots. The so-called justice and salute of war is just a momentary illusion left in this miserable space.

Countless small black dots still returned to the ground, and then flowers painted red and white with people's brains and blood bloomed on the ground.

The transport team composed of civilians and camels was soon scattered by those flocks of "mountain birds." They ran everywhere, trampling on the ice and snow, trampling on human blood. Steamed buns, pancakes, artillery shells and bullets were all abandoned along the way. The soldiers in the trenches were still holding their guns empty-handed, holding a handful of blood-stained snow when they were thirsty; gnawing on a piece of dry food that had already frozen into ice when they were hungry.

Our soldiers are frozen and starving in the snow, in the blood. What are they waiting for? The order of the superior: only defense is allowed, no offense is allowed, so wait, flocks of mountain birds came to "lay eggs" again, and they feasted on these things, dying in the snow, dying in the blood.

Hundreds of thousands of troops were living sacrifices to enemy planes; countless people became victims. Mountains, ponds, cities... in a short period of time, they all changed color completely!

The Chinese planes that we were looking forward to in our dreams, really took off creaking in the air one day at dawn. The people of the whole city were encouraged and joyful, but it didn't take long for them to fall silent again.

The general had already fled on his own plane.

From that time onwards, except for the fact that the security zone was particularly prosperous, the rest of the place was almost covered with a deathly silence. After being silent for more than a month, it is now prosperous everywhere again, and the degree of prosperity is almost impossible to count...

Securities and Twenty-Two Customs Tariff Fall Sharply 234

| Other Areas Also Weak and Listless |

Yesterday, at the Chinese Securities Exchange, the market continued to be in a state of sluggish trading. Market sentiment was extremely sluggish, with supply exceeding demand. In addition, the rush to sell No. 46 and No. 48 twenty-two-year customs tariffs made people feel even more uncertain. Judging from the situation of the market hovering and brewing, it seemed to have a trend of turning smaller. Although the salt tax once approached 53 yuan four times in the morning, it still did not break through. However, the amount of its pullback was also very limited. Therefore, the surface weakness was combined with firmness, evolving into a hovering situation. For the time being, there may not be any major storms, but if the hovering lasts too long, its changes will inevitably be relatively large. Yesterday's transactions were still sluggish, and buyers were not enthusiastic. The only ones that could be mentioned were Nos. 2, 5, and 11, etc., which had relatively more purchases, but at the same time, the selling volume from the sellers was even stronger. No. 46 also had twenty-two-year customs tariffs sold. Although the market price at the opening and closing differed by three points, the difference between the front and back was as much as seven jiao, with the market price opening at 61 yuan, then immediately dropping to 0.05 jiao, and finally closing at 0.03 jiao. It can be seen that the number of actual goods sold must have been large. Then, No. 48 sold, and although there were buyers in the market, it ultimately appeared weak and unable to rise. Therefore, in the two morning sessions and the afternoon opening session, each session generally had a pullback of two or three jiao. The twenty-two-year tariff, because it had not seen the previous price made before opening for many days, fell sharply by one yuan, failing to stabilize. Among them, although No. 16 bought forward disarmament, it once raised the price by two jiao. The nineteen-year customs duty still showed no improvement. Later, because the market slightly covered short positions, starting from the forward twenty-year customs duty, it slightly recovered by one or two jiao. However, No. 6 still remained small by about one jiao due to oversupply. In summary, there is currently no improvement, and the market price results mostly continued to fall by one or two jiao to about half a yuan. Only the twenty-two-year customs tariff fell by one yuan three jiao to two yuan. The total transaction volume was 7,863,000 yuan, including 3,000 yuan in spot goods and 7,860,000 yuan in futures. Under the Control of Monetary Policy

New York Stock Market Extremely Chaotic 235

A report from Sin Fung & Co. on the 5th stated that the New York stock market still lacks change. First, because Roosevelt's speech hinted that he favored increasing wages and reducing working hours, Wall Street believed that this would reduce corporate profits, so the market was sluggish all day. Later, there were rumors that the government would soon raise the price of gold to save prices from falling sharply. Holmes Stock Gold Mine shares soared by 20 yuan. According to reports, the silver faction plans to force the government to mint silver coins, and silver mine shares rose quite strongly. Market sentiment then turned firm. The small exchange lacked buyers, and the market was slightly weak. Bonds were strong due to the strength of foreign public bonds. The total transaction volume for the day was only 950,000 shares. (Wheat) Lacked buyers, and speculators sold slightly loosely. It can be seen that the supply has been drastically reduced, and the Northwest will soon be severely cold. (Cotton) The activities of raising gold prices and the silver faction have a stabilizing effect, but factory purchases are not enthusiastic, speculation is sluggish, and old bulls are tired of selling. Fertilizer sales have increased sharply. At high prices, more selling has increased in the South, and the market seems to be very high temporarily. In addition, this firm received a report from New York Standard Statistics Company that stock prices are down eight yuan from their February peak. There will be no significant changes in the recent period, but the profits of various companies will inevitably show significant progress in the spring. Therefore, the fierce rise of industrial stocks and railway stocks at that time can be predicted. At this time of divergence, what should be paid attention to is selling bad securities and purchasing more promising ones, or holding large sums of money and waiting for opportunities. Interest rates will remain low, so high-grade bonds and government bonds are still good. Although the market occasionally pulls back and the political and monetary atmosphere is often chaotic, the general progress of industry and commerce has shown a glimmer of dawn, so the stock market in the spring can indeed be optimistic. Recent developments in Washington, such as re-estimation, are also sufficient to support the correctness of this statement. The Dow Jones Index is listed below:

Rumors of Grain Truck Stops Raise Future Flour Prices 243

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices for each month generally showed a hovering trend. The quoted price of foreign wheat from Chicago was about one jiao lower, and the quoted price from Canada was four fen lower. Therefore, after the opening price, the market atmosphere for each month was generally flat, and buying and selling were also sluggish. Therefore, the market price was similar to the previous day. Until the afternoon opening, the opening price for each month suddenly turned positive. It was rumored that some large factories were stopping production due to flour inventory. At the same time, it was also rumored that the quoted price of Argentine wheat had risen, recently opening at 4 yuan 2.5 jiao. Therefore, this month gradually increased. Distant months also rose slightly because the factory code was not released. If customer sales are good later, there is still a trend of further improvement in the near term. As a result, this month was up 1.5 fen from the previous day, April was up 1.5 fen, May was up 1.25 fen, June was up 1.5 fen, and July and August were up 1 fen.

Future and Spot Wheat Transactions Are Both Sluggish 244

Yesterday, after the opening of the future wheat market in the morning and afternoon, the prices for each month generally showed a stable trend. However, transactions for each month were still very sluggish. Only a few cars were opened this month in the afternoon. Although the price has not been opened for several days due to factory support, it has improved by nearly a jiao compared to the beginning of the week. Transactions for distant months were also sluggish, and there was no change in price. It was found that the situation in the wheat market, in the old goods stalls, the in and out may not be very large. It must be when there is certainty about the new wheat that it can be lively. Spot wheat transactions were also sluggish. Only 200 bags of Shandong wheat were opened, with a price of 3 yuan 5 jiao.

Hakka Xian Rice Sales to Fujian Gangs Are Still Acceptable 245

11,000 Bags Opened Throughout the Day

Yesterday, the situation of Hakka Xian rice was that some goods from the road arrived in Shanghai, and the owners sought to sell them. The market was mostly medium and secondary grades, and the selling intention was particularly active. After the opening of the market in the morning, all grades below the middle grade fell by five or six fen, and high-grade goods also leveled off slightly. Then, the local street slightly inquired, and Quanzhou and Fuzhou purchased at the reduced market price. However, the current market price in Fujian Province has not risen, and there are also direct shipments from various routes. Therefore, although the appetite is active, the purchase price is very tight. The city opened a total of 11,030 bags of Hunan and Jiangxi rice, of which 900 bags of brown rice went from Ningbo to Hankou, 850 bags of Hunan machine millet from the local street to Jing, more than 500 bags of brown red rice, and more than 400 bags of Jiangxi machine late and machine yuan rice. The rest were all purchased by Quanzhou and Fuzhou in Fujian Province. Fuzhou had a better appetite, with an estimated 5,000 bags going there, and Quanzhou had 2,300 to 2,400 bags going there. The market was weak but revived, still similar to the previous market. Market conditions: High-grade goods have not changed, and medium-grade goods have been balanced by three or four fen.

Woolen Cloth of Medium Thickness is Scarce and Sought After 246

Medium-thick serge is a fast-selling product for Western clothing gangs. Therefore, even though the Hanling stick is popular, the sales of medium-thick serge are still extensive and the English high-grade serge does not fade. English and Americans on warships also often specify it. Most of the ordinary clothing consumers use blue and white edges and Tianyou No. 1000, No. 2000, and Dongfang No. 3008 and other brands. Recently, except for the dismantling shops in Hongkou that have high-grade thick serge, the ordinary goods in the Qipan Street area are very scarce. This is because the arrivals and stocks are not abundant, and the market sales are active, so the supply does not meet the demand. Therefore, yesterday the market atmosphere turned firm. Brands such as Tianyou No. 1000 and No. 2000 were all sold at 5 yuan 2.5 jiao, Dongfang No. 3008 was 5 yuan 1 jiao, Ningfeng Ruyitu was 4 yuan 7.5 jiao, and Deji Foreign Beauty was 5 yuan 2.5 jiao.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Random Talk

Modern Crisis 271

— Qi Su

A huge barrel stands on the current system, so sturdy that it's impossible to find even a tiny leak. People with round bellies take out two large bowls of water from the barrel every day; but at the same time, they pour in five bowls, so the barrel gradually fills up. Much water cannot stand firm inside the barrel, is squeezed out, shouting and climbing around the barrel. This phenomenon, some call it "overproduction," and those squeezed out are the "unemployed."

There are more and more of these people. Society is filled with these dregs, like fallen leaves in autumn, making it impossible to arrange a place for them! And there are many people who were born too late; when they hurriedly crawl out of their "mother's womb," society is already jammed. So they have no chance to enjoy human life, grow up in a harsh environment, without education, without kindness, and without any so-called personality. They don't know what is called thought, called nobility, called harmfulness, only know how to live for immediate pleasure. Anyway, effort is the same, messing around is the same, messing around is the same.

There are a frightening number of these people in Shanghai! Every street, every alley, has their footprints, all places where they seek temporary indulgence. "Stalking," "fighting," "extortion" are their lives. "Chu na" is an indispensable word in their vocabulary. "The body isn't rented, fighting doesn't need learning" is their view of life. "As long as you're ruthless, you can take advantage" is their philosophy. They are always muddle-headed, like flies in June, flying everywhere.

This disease is gradually affecting schools. Bold students glare at them! Cowardly students avoid them, and some are opportunistic? For the sake of convenience in all aspects, the opportunistic ones join forces with them. After all, there are many opportunistic ones! Students are also hanging around with them. Students have become ruffians. Isn't this the most terrifying and widespread phenomenon in recent years?

So the gentlemen sighed. The scholars became agitated. On the imposing lecture platform, in the exquisite reception rooms, at the luxurious banquets, they raise their arms and shout, "This is too bad! This is too bad!" If this continues, how can the country not be weak? How can the great powers not steadily advance and occupy it? They think this is all because the people of the country don't pay enough attention to spiritual training and moral cultivation. Oh! Promote national salvation through spirituality! Oh! Sacred spirit! Hardship, endurance, kindness, universal love, patience, progress, upwardness, bravery, simplicity, integrity, incorruptibility…

But gentlemen and scholars who are used to comfort, don't be fooled by some nice-sounding names! If spirituality could really save the country, our ancient country, which has cultivated spirituality for thousands of years, would never have come to this point. What is spirit? Bombs, airplanes, cannons, that is the true spirit of today's society with its mask removed! "If someone slaps your left cheek, then offer them your right cheek." Can that really move people? That was a long, long time ago. If it had bones, the bones would have turned into minerals long ago, and the minerals would have been used up long ago.

Noble gentlemen! You have sharp fingernails, but you should also have keen eyes! See the bottom of things, dig out the roots, listen to the background of things, find out the truth.

Those people with protruding bellies are taking out two bowls and pouring in five bowls!

The Art of Sleeping (Part 1) 272

— Yi Lu

Regarding sleeping, I remember a scientist who used inductive reasoning to prove the importance of sleeping.

His proof is that everyone has to sleep every night.

This scientist also said, "Sleeping time accounts for at least one-third of people's lifespan." In addition, he further enlightened us: when sleeping, we should pay attention to the time, temperature, and posture, and be careful not to hinder health and benefit the body.

At that time, after listening to this scientist's words, I felt like I had learned more than reading books for ten years. I admired him so much that I wanted to submit a student application to worship him as a teacher, to put in some effort in the science of sleeping, in order to seek deeper knowledge. But I am a lazy fool by nature, and I am most afraid of being managed, and science is the best at managing people. If I worshipped him as a teacher and didn't study diligently and transformed into something that was neither a donkey nor a horse, a "neither-nor," wouldn't that embarrass my teacher?

"Each person sweeps the snow from their own doorstep, and doesn't worry about the frost on other people's roofs." As long as you think it suits your taste, it's better to do things your own way. So when I sleep, I still sleep one or two hours more than ordinary people. I still cover myself with one and a half more quilts than ordinary people. I still sleep with my head covered, lying on my left side or flat on my back - everything is still the same as before. As for the scientist's words, they went in through the right ear and came out through the left ear. From then on, I never thought about the science of sleeping again. And so, another two years have passed.

In total, sleeping like this, sleeping, until now, I have slept for twenty-four three hundred and sixty-five nights. In these twenty-four three hundred and sixty-five nights, I have understood some of the beauty and comfort of sleeping. I feel that sleeping should also be considered an art. As for art, I seem to have heard such a saying: "Even if a person's every move, anything that they think is extraordinary and can enrich their life, from a certain point of view, it can be said to be an art."... Here, a physiologist suddenly angrily said, "You don't understand art at all, but you want to talk about art, you're defiling art; according to you, then shitting, pissing, and farting all have to be called art? Ridiculous! Ridiculous!" This gentleman is really nosy. I'm writing my own things, why does he have to nag: "Tell me the reasons why sleeping is art!" I should reply: "How dare I? How dare I? Please calm down, and allow me to explain it in detail:"

"In the large and small Western-style houses on Jing'an Temple Road, Foch Road, or Gordon Road, Seymour Road, Yuyuan Road, etc., the faint electric light shines through the snow-white纱 curtains from the windows, reflecting the murky winter sky, the piano in the room resonates with both solemn and melodious (one) (two) (three) (four) (five) sounds, and the lullabies from the radio, vaguely, wave after wave, reach the ears of pedestrians on the road. If you are a thoughtful person, you might as well walk slowly along these roads, take out a cigarette, strike a match, and slowly smoke and think. Think about what the owners of those Western houses are doing, and experience their taste, it will really make you want to think more and more, so much so that you don't even realize that the cigarette in your mouth is burning your lips, that's enough to make your soul truly inverted! Look, do you see? Doesn't it seem like a magnificent and exquisite bedroom is appearing before your eyes? Look, aren't the silver frames hanging on the walls decorated with light yellow plaster all paintings of foreign women? Isn't the floor covered with thick and soft carpets? Isn't it plum blossoms in full bloom on the flower stand? Aren't all the furnishings in the room comfortable and beautiful? Also, in the center of the room! What is standing there, burning red, if not an electric heater? The radio that is playing in front of the bedside table! Do you see? Isn't a middle-aged man with a face full of smiles sitting in the bed, his legs already stretched into the quilt, his upper body wearing a wool pajama leaning against the headboard? One hand is holding a book and reading, and the other hand is holding a cigar between two fingers. The radio is still playing, playing. The man listens intently, sometimes closing his eyes like this, sometimes picking up his cigar and taking a puff. Suddenly, the head of the bed moved a little, and a head poked out from the quilt - a woman's head! I didn't see it at first, there was still a beautiful woman sleeping in the bed under the quilt. How soul-stirring! (To be continued)

The Story of a Street Urchin (1) 273

— Chen Sheng

Lili is a lovely child. Her younger brother is missing.

Female Writer Ya Fei 274

—

In modern society, almost everything has become commodified! Art and literature are of course things to earn a living, and in the end, they cannot escape commodified competition. Nowadays, even personality is being auctioned off!

Recently, a female writer: in order to "understand society," went to "try a new life" (as she herself said), so she did not hesitate to run into an XXX dance hall to work as a dancer. I imagine this female writer; is at least great, brave. Since she herself declared: "This is because she felt that life had no meaning, and went to try this new life"... then there is no doubt, she did not come here for economic reasons, for life. But I think; being a dancer is still a profession, not a noble profession, a profession of being hugged and embraced by others; using beauty, using smiles, using... to earn money. Those dancers who are oppressed by the environment and driven by life; we should already sympathize with them, pity them. Because they are struggling under the claws of demons! Perhaps hot tears will drip from their welcoming smiles. Otherwise, who would really be willing to do this kind of night life that sells the soul, sells the body, and is played with by others? This is for money, money calls them to do it, and they think so, this is a degenerate business, this is an inhuman life. They want to be a young mistress, grandmother, or even a wife, ride in a car, live in a Western-style house, how happy. But fate controls their reality.

Now this female writer; actually boldly goes to try the life of a dancer, which is equivalent to selling the body, her only ambition is "to understand society." It is true that the deformed complexity of modern society cannot be denied by anyone, but if you want to understand society, you must deeply understand the situation and organization of modern society, and make a detailed observation. Like an explorer, run into the steep and dangerous deep mountains and jungles to experience it firsthand. Then, I naturally also hope, like the departure of an explorer, that this female writer will return with great gains. But, pitifully, what she tried was only the life of a dancer. If she were willing to go a step further and try to approach more of the upper, middle, and lower societies, I believe that her understanding of society would be truly thorough.

However, I always feel somewhat suspicious about her? If she simply said, for life, for the economy, then we should of course not criticize her, but also sympathize with her. Because being a dancer is still a profession, and professions are inherently non-noble, without class. Now she insists on saying that it is "trying a new life," and for "wanting to understand society." But, I think that this is inevitably somewhat opportunistic! If she really wants to "understand society," then I want to advise her to do... here, it is easier to approach society than being a dancer, and it is easier to experience all the dark and bright sides of society, people, and life.

How resounding is the name of a writer. Having the title of a writer is like ascending the Dragon Gate, and your worth increases tenfold. However, sometimes there are people who go to sell writers, sell the personality of writers!

Unfortunate Caged Bird 275

— Zi

Rong wrote from Beiping, and the first sentence said that Xiong committed suicide in Beihai last month. The reason is written on the stationery like this:

We not only grieve for Xiong, but we should also be indignant for him! Although he has not made any contributions to society, he has already vowed to dedicate himself; but society is cruelly ruthless to him! This was still during the summer vacation last year, when he graduated from university. He didn't think that wearing a square hat would increase his worth. He was just secretly happy that he had reached a stage in his studies, and could serve society from now on. At that time, he was really burning with the flame of life, enthusiastically advancing on the journey of life. But, in this society, he didn't know that he was a poor boy without wealthy relatives, where was his place? Where was there something for him to do? So he ran from Beiping to Tianjin, from Tianjin to Shanghai. He lived in Shanghai for two months. Later, he told me that he had forgotten where you lived, so he never had a chance to see you. I think this was his fatal injury, because if he could find you, you could help him a little, and wouldn't let him run around on the wide, smooth roads for two months in vain. In his suicide note, it is said that he was not discouraged at that time, and he was still ambitiously going to create a gold mountain of career in his ideal. The seed of his suicide this time was planted when he left Shanghai for Guangzhou, and failing to get anything, from Guangzhou to Nanchang; in Nanchang, he still achieved nothing, so he began to curse life. He listened without any control to the encouragement of an unrelated fellow villager. Finally, he drifted to his hometown, hometown, a hometown that was bankrupt and collapsed, how could it be the location of his gold mountain of career? Of course, this was nothing more than reducing his courage to be a human being. At the beginning of the month, he suddenly ran here to see me, saying that his affairs were all resolved. At that time, I thought that he had really found a job, and I was enthusiastically congratulating him. How could I know that he was solving his problems by dying? In his suicide note, he said, "Anyway, Beiping is the place that made me a vagrant, so I might as well die in Beiping." He also explained, "If I had given up struggling these last four years, I believe society wouldn't have abandoned me like this." How sad and painful this must be!...

I trembled, holding the letter high and silently reading it, and the face of a lively and happy young man appeared in my mind. His strong and tall figure, sincere and enthusiastic temperament, especially the pair of dark, sharp eyes deeply sunken under his thick eyebrows, revealed great wisdom. Usually, he was always worried that the education of the ancient Chinese nation was not enough, and he vowed to put the great task of revitalization on his own shoulders, so although he was poor, he wanted to go to school to study. Every semester, he desperately borrowed from friends, for four years, he struggled so hard, but he was always happy and optimistic, because in his ideal, there really existed a "gold mountain of career," and he was also very confident in this.

Xiong is dead, of course I want to grieve for him, and like Rong, express indignation at this society! However, Xiong's own words in his suicide note are ultimately reasonable, "If I had given up struggling these last four years..." How profound and painful this must be!

Here, we have an understanding of the existing traditional education: schools are like a birdcage, a delicate and beautiful birdcage, although the bird's owner has arranged rockeries and artificial rocks inside, and there are also precious and delicious foods, but the bird students are ultimately separated from the real mountains and real rocks in nature. Their line of thought is ultimately circling the rockeries and artificial rocks in this delicate and beautiful cage. Once they leave the cage and return to nature, they undoubtedly feel lost, and even lose the instinct to fly! We know how cruel and sinful this birdcage is! However, destroying this birdcage must be done by the birds themselves.

Modern Celebrities' Calligraphy and Painting 276

— Mr. Mu Yilong's Jin Hui Xiong (from Shanghai)

Fiction

Lulu's Victory (4) 277

— Written by Italian M Serao, Translated by Jing Xin

She opened the door, letting her mother and sister walk out, bowing deeply, and whispering; "Madam, Miss!" When they walked out of the house, she laughed loudly at them at the door and shouted:

"You just go ahead and talk, I'll pretend I don't know anything."

Normally, Robert. Montfort Lanco. He is not a very thoughtful person; he is not enough to become a thinker. His life is banquets, riding horses, and visitors; his nights are spent happily with his fiancée Lulu. Then there are the troublesome matters that need to be handled, appointments with his lawyer, the signing of certain contracts, the resolution of some existing claims, and many other annoying things, such as his family and his honeymoon. He hardly has half an hour to read, no fifteen minutes to stop at a coffee shop, so we never see him immersed in deep thought, and we never see him engaged in solving any social problems, because there is no such heroic or tragic temperament in Robert's character. His temperament can rather be said to be calm, and many people are therefore jealous of him.

But on this day in the afternoon, he leaned back in his armchair, one leg crossed over the other, concentrating on reading. The book was quite interesting; but it was a bit novel, which made the reader absent-minded. In fact, he was not just absent-minded; he was restless and a little nervous. He hadn't turned a page, because just after reading two lines, the words printed on the page seemed to be jumping, unreadable, and disappearing. Robert naturally entered a realm of thought he had never experienced before.
