Movie Special

Regarding the Production of Aviation Films (Continued) 278

— Ling Zhen

In aviation film combat scenes, most are filmed using two or more aircraft. The aircraft carrying the actors is equipped with machine guns, and after the actors are seated inside and fly up, they begin acting, as if the bullets fired from their machine guns are hitting enemy aircraft. At this time, there are aircraft following him on his left and right sides. Inside these left and right aircraft sit the director and cameraman, who are there filming the actor's performance. When both sides have captured the actor's performance, it is as if the scenes were not performed at the same time, because the positioning of the cameras is different, so the scenes they film are also different. Then, by selectively using scenes from these different positions, many scenes can be created. This is a convenient method, but the machine gun firing scenes must never be filmed head-on towards the camera, because if the machine gun muzzle is aimed at the camera and fired, not only will the scene not be filmed, but the cameraman's life will be lost.

We can also see the aircraft seemingly flying straight towards us, about to reach us and then suddenly flying upwards and away. This is also a very difficult scene to film. To film this scene, a camera is mounted on one aircraft to film another aircraft. The aircraft being filmed flies straight towards the aircraft with the camera. Just as they are about to collide, the filmed aircraft flies past the aircraft with the camera. When shown in the film, it looks like the aircraft is flying straight towards us, about to reach us, and then suddenly flying upwards.

When actors are filming aviation scenes, if they feel slightly unwell, they should not be forced to fly into the sky. Forcing themselves to act on the ground is still possible, but not in the sky. A sick actor flying into the sky can make their illness worse. Therefore, before filming an aviation film, every staff member and actor must be very healthy to prevent accidents.

Some thrilling scenes in aviation films are made using rephotography. In our eyes, it looks like a very thrilling event has occurred in the sky, but during filming, it is not necessarily very dangerous. Some scenes are filmed outdoors first, and then brought back to the company's glass studio for re-filming, using reprinting methods to ensure that no flaws are revealed. When you watch it, you still think it was filmed safely in the sky. Some are also filmed using models. This is the same as using models in ordinary films. If the cameraman's movements and camera panning are appropriate, you will definitely not be able to tell that it is a model. Lighting is very important when filming aviation films. Although it is entirely using sunlight, the cameraman must use the light well to increase the power of the drama.

The editing of aviation films is also very important. If an aviation film is edited well, it can provide many tense scenes that give you a powerful stimulation. Otherwise, the thrilling scenes filmed with a lot of effort, money, and great difficulty and danger will not feel thrilling at all when you watch them. Therefore, aviation films must not only pay attention to cinematography, but also to the editing work.

The production of aviation films is not an easy task, it is much more difficult than filming ordinary films. (The End)

Film Reviews

Review of "I Lived With You" 279

— Ling He

I Lived With You

丨Lanxin Guanglu丨

I think this kind of story is not entirely without meaning. When the wandering Grand Duke sold two diamonds from a watch bestowed upon him by Emperor Nicholas, it caused conflict and unease in the family. The father stole half of the proceeds, while the mother regarded him as an honored guest and boasted about him to the neighbors. The elder sister fell in love with him, and the younger sister also wanted to take him for herself, all because he had once been a glorious Grand Duke and possessed the valuable diamonds on the watch.

Here, it can be proven that the playwright, Luo Faluo, truly has experience in human affairs. He not only uses jewels to increase the conflict in a seemingly happy family, but he even makes them lose their reason. These are very realistic phenomena, regardless of whether only an exiled Grand Duke can achieve this. Of course, the playwright later develops his own ideals; he does not allow the Grand Duke to further destroy the family's happiness, but teaches him to resolutely leave the family. However, in order to make people sympathize with the Grand Duke's kindness, he ultimately allows the passionate Gedaisi to follow him, saying that she is following him out of love to live a simple life.

Precisely because of this, we can see the playwright's entire ideology. Perhaps Luo Faluo wrote the play entirely for his own starring role, so in many scenes, he tries his best to express himself. In particular, the ups and downs of the love between the protagonist and Gedaisi are written vividly. Therefore, he takes such material, conceiving an exiled Grand Duke in his ideal. In the unique personality of being romantic, suave, and self-sacrificing, he allows himself to be able to exert himself to the utmost when starring.

But any material, when we adopt it, must be chosen through our own thinking. Then Luo Faluo uses the characters of the old Russian royal family as his own stand-ins, and also vigorously sympathizes with him; this is by no means accidental, but fully reflects his own ideology. Perhaps some people will say that he does not have any obvious insults to the current Russian government in the play, and even in the dialogue, he does not curse the revolution in any way. However, rather than saying that he is standing in the position of a third party and not involving himself in politics, it is better to say that he cannot and dare not do so. Moreover, he wants the audience to sympathize with the fate of the royal family, even if it is sentimental, this has already given people a bad impression.

As mentioned above, Luo Faluo wrote the play entirely for himself, so his performance is indeed worthy of praise. It goes without saying that he can act calmly, and his delicate performance is even more commendable. In his performance, we can see that he has full cultivation, and even the slightest movement reveals a wealth of emotion.

However, it is no exaggeration to say that the only commendable aspect of this film is his performance. In addition, the actress who plays the mother also performs extremely well. When she boasts to her neighbors in the vegetable market, and when she immediately bursts into loud weeping when she suffers a temporary setback, we can see a deep understanding of the character in the play. Furthermore, the actress who plays Gedaisi is also very good. The actress who plays Mrs. Felix's cousin gives us a serious impression.

Naturally, if we consider this work not to be a failure, then the director deserves considerable credit. Regarding this aspect of the review, other than the introduction of the identities and professions of those individuals at the beginning being not economical enough, all other scenes are very refined. Naturally, the gag on the female cook proves that British films will tend to be first-class with American films, but this is also the best way to reconcile the dullness; for example, the two sitting together several times is a long conversation, which is necessary to regulate. However, like the Grand Duke not bathing and making the sound of bathing, this can both depict the Grand Duke's laziness and is a very interesting scene.

Other than that, there is nothing else to say. This is a rare comedy with a touch of tragedy among a series of British comedies, although it does not have any particular value.

"Gold Diggers of the Sky" to be Released Soon 280

— Yun

While every film company is vying to produce musical films, RKO naturally is not willing to lag behind and is also working hard on this type of product. "Gold Diggers of the Sky" is its first and last musical film. In terms of style and conception, it does have distinct differences. First, it moves the grand musical scenes to the great sky, and transforms the footing of hundreds of beautiful girls to the wings of airplanes. While the airplanes soar in the sky, the beauties dance on the wings. Second, the ground musical troupe emphasizes artistry. There is a very exquisite tango dance, and teams of dancing dolls advance and retreat at a measured pace with the music. In particular, a poetic love song "Carioca." The singing will make anyone's heart sway and be unable to control themselves. The protagonists of the film are Dolores del Río and Gene Raymond. The director is Thornton Freeland. His past work "Flying Down to Rio" once swept across the entire Shanghai. The film has already been booked by the Grand Shanghai Theatre and will be released in the shortest possible time. (Paid Contribution)

Three Anecdotes from Tianyi

— Xiaoren

Zhang Zhentuo Wants to Jump into the Huangpu River 281

The villain Zhang Zhentuo purchased a fourth-term aviation lottery ticket with the number "324509." It happened to differ from the first prize "324504" by only the last digit. On the day of the draw, Zhang saw the first prize number in the evening newspaper, which truly infuriated him. He didn't even eat dinner and talked incoherently into the night, shouting that he wanted to jump into the Huangpu River. His wife has been carefully watching over him day and night for the past two days, fearing that he might actually throw himself into the Huangpu River!

Shao Suxia Takes Strange Photos 282

Child star Shao Suxia recently bought a small camera. It is exquisite, small, and has a beautiful design. However, because she is a beginner in photography, the results are very poor. Yesterday, she took half a dozen photos with Guan Dafangzi in the sunlight. Guan Fatty was very happy and prepared to send a copy to his beloved wife after they were developed. However, after the photos were developed, they either lacked a nose and ears, or had a mouth but no eyes, or were even invisible. None of the six photos looked like a person, which infuriated Guan Fatty so much that the fat on his face kept trembling. He exclaimed that he had bad luck this year.

Wei Pengfei's Weasel Mourns for the Rabbit 283

The old man Wei Pengfei, although nearly fifty years old, is as physically strong as a robust young man. Wei recently became acquainted with a Guangdong woman who is thirty-eight years old, beautiful, and skilled in poetry and prose. Therefore, Wei is very fond of her. Every day, as soon as he finishes work at the company, he goes straight home. As a result, he no longer has the heart to feed the several beloved white rabbits he keeps at the company. The day before yesterday, Wei suddenly remembered that he had not fed the rabbits for many days. He rushed to the rabbit hutch and found it empty. Only bloodstains and several piles of leftover bones could be seen on the ground. It was clear that the rabbits had been eaten by weasels. Wei couldn't help but shed tears at this tragic sight. At this time, Ge Erkuaitou (Note: Ge Erkuaitou is Ge Furong. Ge was originally Tianyi's number one fatty, but since Guan Hongda joined Tianyi, Ge could no longer monopolize the title of fatty, so he had to settle for second place) was standing next to him and said silently: "Old Wei, don't be a weasel mourning for the rabbit, go home and see your wife." (Paid Contribution)

George Brent's Masterpiece "The Purchase Price" | Showing in Nanjing 284

George Brent, the big star who portrays "heroic types," is now meeting with Shanghai audiences on the screen again. This film focuses on depicting life in the lower strata, satirizing the corruption of the American judicial system, and exposing the various forms of social pathology and decadent life. It can be said to be incisive. The mutual pursuit mania between men and women and the various frustrations of life are also fully propagated, and it can be called an unprecedented blockbuster, and a great contribution of United Artists Corporation of America.

The female lead is played by Francis Dee, who plays a delicate and charming socialite, while Marian Nixon plays a sentimental heroine, and the heroine's younger brother is played by Chick Chandler.

The Honor and Glory of a White Mouse 285

— Fu

Everyone probably still remembers that hot girl Clara Bow has a white mouse, the one she went to New York and forgot to bring, and then specially sent a plane to pick up. Now that mouse is dead, and Clara even shed a lot of tears for it, because she had been feeding it for five years, and they can be said to be dependent on each other. When the mouse died, many of her friends, knowing her grief, found many small animals, such as badger cubs, guinea pigs, and parrots, and sent them to her, but she could not change her mood and mourn, and she said to everyone she met: "Pinky" (small mouse nickname) is dead, nothing in the world can replace it!

Film Novel

The Scarlet Empress Catherine the Great 286

— Sumei

A Paramount Production Directed by Josef von Sternberg Starring Marlene Dietrich

Almost two hundred years ago, in a corner of Prussia, there was a young and beautiful woman, a princess, spending her leisurely years, unaware that her future destiny would be to become the Empress of Russia. This petite and delicate woman was Princess Sophia Frederica, still a naive young girl. She had a small oval face, eyes as blue as the sky, and hair curls that shone like gold. Her petite body was full of exuberant youthful vitality. The world she knew was only the realm of love. She loved her nanny, Kadul, and also her teacher, Wagner. She also loved her young and beautiful mother, Princess Johanna, but she did not know her mother's ambitions and ruthless plans for her. She especially respected her father. Her father, Prince August, was older than her mother and was a very loving, wise, and experienced man. She also loved one thing, which was her old doll. Although she was past the age of playing with dolls, she still often slept with it, telling it her happy dreams in bed.

How different were Sophia's dreams from those of her mother! Princess Johanna often told her that she would become an Empress in the future. But what did Sophia secretly imagine? Just a ballerina! As for mentioning Russia, that strange country far away in the far north, Sophia only knew some of it from what Wagner painstakingly taught her from books 丨丨What Peter the Great, what Ivan the Terrible, all were cruel and overbearing tsars 丨丨There were also Cossack soldiers as fierce as beasts and oppressed and groaning commoners. In Sophia's innocent and tender mind, none of these were real, just some stories in books that would be forgotten after reading. How could real people be like this?

But in Johanna's heart, the throne of Russia was real. She was moving her pieces, thinking deeply and carefully. One day, the Russian envoy arrived. Sophia's father called her to introduce the Russian Emperor's ambassador, Duke Alexei. Alexei had come to welcome her and her mother to Moscow. Her visit to Russia was to marry the Russian Grand Duke, Peter Fyodorovich. Peter Fyodorovich was the grandson of Peter the Great and the nephew of the Russian Empress Elizabeth, and he was going to inherit the throne in the future. Duke Alexei was young, and he was a little stunned when he saw how beautiful Sophia was. He slowly said, "Your Highness, Princess, although people in our country have long heard of your beauty, but really. I wasn't prepared to see such elegance." After he finished speaking, he bowed and kissed Sophia's slender jade hand. (To be continued)
